### [40] [GEMS: Geometric Constraints Enable Multi-Semantic Superposition in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19946)
*Yu Deng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型多方向激活干预导致的模型崩溃问题，本文提出了GEMS方法，通过实时正交化和分布控制技术，实现了在不重训模型的情况下，稳定、精确地控制模型的多种行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的激活引导（Activation Steering）技术主要处理单向注入。当尝试叠加多个语义方向时，由于分布偏移（范数累积导致的激活超出训练范围）和方向干扰（非正交向量间的相互削弱），模型极易崩溃。因此，需要研究多方向干预的约束机制。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为GEMS的训练无关方法，包含两个核心几何约束：1. 针对分布偏移的范数保持加权叠加与目标注意力路径注入；2. 针对方向干扰的实时正交化处理。

Result: 在GSM8K测试中，GEMS方法实现了三路非数学方向的并发注入，准确率保持在98%（基准为92%，未加约束叠加则崩溃至4%）；在Wikitext-2数据集上，困惑度（PPL）仅增加2.2%。实验证明该方法在不同规模（3B至31B）模型间具有良好的迁移性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的GEMS方法通过几何约束有效解决了多方向激活干预中的模型崩溃问题，证明了在不改变模型权重的前提下，可以精确控制大语言模型的多种行为，为模型行为可控性研究提供了理论框架和实用方案。

Abstract: Activation steering controls model behavior by modifying intermediate hidden states at inference time without retraining. Existing methods handle only single-direction injection; when multiple semantic directions are superposed without constraints, the model collapses. We show that this collapse decomposes into two independently acting sources: distributional deviation, where additive perturbations accumulate in norm across layers and drive activations outside the training distribution, and directional interference, where non-orthogonal semantic vectors mutually dampen when superposed. These two sources define the design constraints that any training-free multi-directional intervention must address. As one instantiation of these principles, we propose GEMS, a training-free method that maps each source to a corresponding geometric constraint: norm-preserving weighted superposition and targeted attention-pathway injection for distributional deviation, and real-time orthogonalization for directional interference. On GSM8K, injecting three concurrent non-mathematical directions preserves accuracy at 98% (baseline 92%), while unconstrained addition collapses to 4%; on Wikitext-2, the same injection incurs only 2.2% PPL increase. Component ablation isolates the causal role of each constraint, and layer-level probes confirm that orthogonalized signals survive the FFN pathway and reach the output distribution with semantic specificity. Qualitative steering effects transfer across architectures from 3B to 31B.

*Sunghee Ahn,Guijin Son,Youngjae Yu*

Abstract: From financial filings to clinical records, legacy industries rely heavily on long, unstructured documents to store high-value information. Reliably extracting this information into structured, machine-readable representations is a key prerequisite to making the contents accessible to automated systems. JSON is a natural target for such structured extraction, yet constructing reliable and scalable text-to-JSON training data remains challenging. To address this gap, we propose STAGE (Spreadsheet-grounded Text-to-JSON Artifact GEneration), a source-grounded data generation pipeline that constructs reports and JSON schema by using LLMs for scalable synthesis while validating ground-truth values against the underlying spreadsheet. Evaluations on STAGE-Eval, our source-grounded benchmark with an 851-example test set, show that STAGE produces stronger training data than existing approaches. This improves Qwen3-4B exact match from 31.37% to 74.27% and value accuracy from 45.46% to 90.69%.

A controlled tokenizer ablation on the IHUBERT pretraining corpus shows that BPE yields slightly lower subword fragmentation than WordPiece at matched vocabulary size, supporting our tokenization design. Overall, IHUBERT advances Persian language modeling through semantically curated large-scale pretraining and broad evaluation across both classification and comprehension-oriented tasks.

### [43] [Self-Preference Is Weak or Absent in Verifiable Instruction-Following Revision: A Four-Model Test Under Genuine Authorship](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20093)
*William Guey,Pierrick Bougault*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究利用IFEval验证器对大模型的自我修订过程进行评估，结果发现模型在面对有效的文本修正时，并不会因为是自己写的就表现出偏袒或拒绝改进，推翻了关于模型存在自我偏好偏见的主流担忧。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型经常被用于内容创作与修订，但人们普遍担心模型在审阅自身文本时会表现出“自我偏好偏见”，即倾向于保护自己先前生成的内容而拒绝有效的改进建议。本研究旨在通过科学实验验证模型是否真的存在这种抗拒修正的行为。

Method: 研究采用了确定性验证器（IFEval）来界定什么是“有效的修正”。实验过程为：首先让模型生成草稿；利用IFEval检查器确认草稿违反了约束，并提供一个能修复该问题的修正方案；随后，分别由模型以“原作者”身份和“中立第三方”身份对该修正进行判断，记录其接受或拒绝的情况。最终对比两组模型的决策差异。

Result: 研究发现，在85次原作者与中立者的对比实验中，未检测到显著的自我偏好倾向。原作者模型拒绝经过验证的有效修正的比例与中立模型几乎相同（差异仅为 -5.1 个百分点）。此外，当作者拒绝修正时，97%的原因是由于模型认为修正存在缺陷，而非出于对原内容的偏好。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在中等规模的模型中，并没有证据支持“大型语言模型在修订自身文本时存在拒绝有效修正的自我偏好（Self-preference bias）”这一假设。模型作为原作者与作为中立评判者时，对有效修正的采纳率基本一致。这意味着模型在自我修订时的决策并非源于对自身生成内容的偏袒。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) increasingly review and revise text, including their own. A documented self-preference bias (models favoring their own generations when acting as judges) raises the question of whether models also resist valid corrections to their own writing. We test this in a setting where "valid" is decided not by another model but by a deterministic verifier: instruction-following revision on IFEval. A model writes a draft; the official IFEval checker confirms the draft violates a constraint and that a candidate edit fixes it; the model then accepts or rejects that edit either as the genuine in-context author or as a fresh model that sees the draft neutrally. Across four mid-tier model families and 85 author-versus-fresh comparisons, we find no detectable self-preference: authors reject verified-good fixes to their own drafts at essentially the same rate as fresh models judging the same drafts (gap -5.1 pp, 95% CI [-12.9, +2.7]). A self-skepticism hint from a smaller pilot did not replicate at scale. The one robust observation is qualitative: when authors do reject a verified-good fix, 97% of their stated reasons are flaw-catching rather than preference, that is, about the character of rejections, not an elevated rate. Effects smaller than ~13 pp cannot be excluded at this sample size.

</details>


### [44] [HydraHead: From Head-Level Functional Heterogeneity to Specialized Attention Hybridization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20097)
*Zhentao Tan,Wei Chen,Jingyi Shen,Yao Liu,Xu Shen,Yue Wu,Jieping Ye*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型注意力计算复杂度的瓶颈，本文提出了 HydraHead 架构。不同于常见的层级混合方案，该方法在“注意力头”维度对全注意力和线性注意力进行精细化融合，通过可解释性驱动的选择策略与尺度归一化技术，在大幅降低长上下文计算成本的同时，显著提升了模型性能与扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型注意力机制存在平方级计算复杂度的瓶颈。虽然层级混合注意力模型已被提出，但 Linear Attention 与 Full Attention 的融合难度较高。研究发现模型层内存在头级功能异质性，即不同头具备不同的功能专长，这为在头维度进行更精细的混合提供了理论依据。

Method: 1. 引入 HydraHead 架构：在注意力头维度而非层级维度混合全注意力（FA）与线性注意力（LA）；
2. 可解释性驱动的头选择策略：识别检索关键头保留 FA，其余使用 LA；
3. 尺度归一化融合模块：解决 FA 与 LA 输出之间的分布差异；
4. 三阶段迁移流程：通过参数重用和蒸馏技术降低训练开销。

Result: 1. 在长上下文任务中表现优于其他混合设计；
2. 仅用 7:1 的 LA 到 FA 比例即可达到传统 3:1 层级混合的效果；
3. 仅使用 15B Token 训练，在 512K 上下文长度任务中较基线提升 69% 以上，性能逼近同等规模的领先模型 Qwen3.5（其原生长度为 256K）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 HydraHead 架构证明了在注意力头维度进行混合（而非传统的层级混合）是一种更有效且具备更高扩展潜力的设计范式。通过精细化的头级注意力选择和分布对齐，模型能在显著降低计算复杂度的同时，在超长上下文处理任务中展现出卓越性能，为构建高效长上下文大模型提供了新的架构思路。

Abstract: The quadratic complexity of attention poses a critical bottleneck for long-context processing, spurring interest in hybrid attention designs. Most open-source hybrid models adopt a layer-wise strategy. Yet, prior work has noted the inherent difficulty of integrating Linear Attention (LA) with Full Attention (FA), suggesting that the design space of attention hybridization remains underexplored. To probe this space, we conduct interpretability analysis and observe that layers exhibit block-wise functional similarity, while individual heads within the same layer display distinct functional specialization despite sharing input features. This head-level heterogeneity suggests that the head dimension provides a natural and principled granularity for fusing heterogeneous attention signals. Building on this insight, we introduce HydraHead, a novel architecture that hybridizes FA and LA along the head axis. HydraHead features two key innovations: (1) an interpretability-driven selection strategy that identifies retrieval-critical heads and preserves FA only for them, and (2) a scale-normalized fusion module that reconciles the distributional gap between FA and LA head outputs. By leveraging a three-stage transfer pipeline with parameter reuse and distillation, we achieve high-performance hybrid models with minimal training overhead. Under a unified training setup, HydraHead outperforms other hybrid designs in long-context tasks while maintaining strong general reasoning. With interpretability-driven head selection, it matches a 3:1 layer-wise hybrid's long-context performance at a 7:1 LA-to-FA ratio. Crucially, trained on only 15B tokens, HydraHead achieves over 69% improvement over the baseline at 512K context length, approaching Qwen3.5, a leading model of comparable size with a native context length of 256K. This highlights the significant scaling potential of head-level hybridization.

</details>


### [45] [From Texts to Scores: Tracing the Emergence of Essay Quality Representations in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20152)
*Jiaxu Zuo,Mu You,Kaixin Lan,Tao Fang,Yujia Huo,Henghua Shen,Lidia S. Chao,Derek F. Wong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了大型语言模型（LLMs）在自动作文评分中的内部机理，证明了LLMs通过线性可解码的方式编码作文质量，并定位了负责评分的关键神经元，为模型的可解释性提供了实证支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在自动作文评分（AES）领域应用广泛，但其内部如何理解和评估作文质量的机制尚不明确，缺乏对其深层表征的系统性研究。

Method: 研究通过线性探测（linear probing）、跨提示词泛化测试、降维分析以及神经元级分析等方法，在8种大型语言模型和3个数据集（ASAP++、CSEE、ENEM）上进行了系统性探究。此外，还通过非线性探测对比及针对性神经元干预实验，验证了评分信息的编码特性。

Result: 研究发现：1. 作文质量信息以线性可访问的形式编码在模型表示中；2. 这些表征在模型层级中表现出渐进式涌现，且具有跨提示词的鲁棒性；3. 非线性探测对比表明大部分信息已是线性可解码的；4. 识别出了与评分高度相关的“作文评分神经元”，且其分布随作文长度变化。

Conclusion: 本文证实了大型语言模型内部确实存在与作文质量相关的结构化表征，这些表征具有线性可分性和跨任务的鲁棒性。研究不仅揭示了模型评估作文的内在机制，还通过定位“评分神经元”为提升自动作文评分（AES）系统的可解释性及性能提供了重要基础。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) have substantially transformed Automated Essay Scoring (AES), yet the internal mechanisms underlying LLM-based scoring remain poorly understood. In this work, we systematically analyze the hidden representations of eight LLMs across two English essay datasets (ASAP++, CSEE) and one Portuguese dataset (ENEM). Using linear probing, cross-prompt generalization, dimensionality reduction, and neuron-level analyses, we find consistent evidence that essay quality information is encoded in a linearly accessible form within LLM representations. These representations emerge progressively across layers, remain robust across prompting strategies, and partially transfer across essay prompts despite differences in scoring rubrics. In addition, nonlinear probes provide only marginal and inconsistent improvements over linear probes, suggesting that most essay quality information is already linearly decodable. We further identify individual ``essay scoring neurons'' whose activations strongly correlate with essay scores and whose behavior is sensitive to targeted intervention. Moreover, the layer-wise distribution of these neurons systematically shifts with essay length, with longer essays relying more heavily on deeper layers. Overall, our findings provide evidence that LLMs encode structured representations related to essay quality and offer new insights into the interpretability of LLM-based AES systems.

### [46] [MedRLM: Recursive Multimodal Health Intelligence for Long-Context Clinical Reasoning, Sensor-Guided Screening, Evidence-Grounded Decision Support, and Community-to-Tertiary Referral Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20164)
*Aueaphum Aueawatthanaphisut*

Conclusion: MedRLM标志着医疗AI从静态问答向可审计、多模态及流程感知的临床决策支持系统的重要转型，能够更有效地处理复杂的临床决策任务。

Abstract: Real-world clinical decision support requires reasoning over heterogeneous and longitudinal patient information rather than answering isolated medical questions. However, current medical large language models and retrieval-augmented generation systems often rely on single-step prompting or retrieval, which can be fragile when clinical evidence is distributed across long electronic health records, medical images, sensor streams, guidelines, and referral constraints. This paper proposes MedRLM, a Recursive Multimodal Health Intelligence framework for long-context clinical reasoning, sensor-guided screening, and community-to-tertiary referral support. Instead of compressing all patient information into one prompt, MedRLM treats the patient case as an external clinical environment that can be recursively inspected, decomposed, retrieved, verified, and synthesized. The framework coordinates specialized agents for clinical text, longitudinal EHR, medical imaging, physiological sensor signals, guideline retrieval, uncertainty auditing, and referral planning. It further introduces a Clinical Evidence Graph Memory to connect patient-specific observations with retrieved evidence, standardized definitions, sensor-derived biomarkers, and referral criteria. A sensor-guided recursive triggering mechanism activates deeper reasoning when abnormal physiological or behavioral patterns are detected, while uncertainty-gated refinement supports clinician review for high-risk or low-confidence cases. We also outline a real-data evaluation design using public and credentialed clinical datasets spanning EHR, radiology, ECG, ICU time series, and referral-proxy outcomes. MedRLM aims to move medical AI from static question answering toward auditable, multimodal, and workflow-aware clinical decision support.

### [47] [ReNikud: Audio-Supervised Hebrew Grapheme-to-Phoneme Conversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20179)
*Maxim Melichov,Yakov Kolani,Morris Alper*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对希伯来语书写缺失元音导致G2P转换困难的问题，研究提出ReNikud模型，利用大规模未标注音频的弱监督学习和强制字符对齐架构，实现了比传统方法更准确、更符合口语发音的音标预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希伯来语作为一种辅音音素文字（Abjad），在书写中省略元音，导致G2P转换存在巨大歧义。传统的加注音符号（Nikud）方法受限于标注数据稀缺、忽略词汇重音以及过于规范化（脱离实际口语），而直接的序列到序列转换模型在有限数据下表现不佳，且未能利用该语言特有的字符对齐特性。

Method: 该研究提出了ReNikud模型，包含两个核心策略：1. 利用基于音素的自动语音识别（ASR）伪标签管道，从数千小时未标注的希伯来语音频中获取弱监督数据，从而捕捉真实的口语发音；2. 采用伪发音架构，在每个字符位置预测IPA音素，通过强制字符级对齐作为归纳偏置，以解决直接序列到序列预测在数据稀疏时的困难。

Result: 在现有的希伯来语G2P基准测试以及针对口语希伯来语新建立的MILIM基准测试中，ReNikud均表现优异，超越了现有的先进技术水平。

Conclusion: ReNikud通过结合弱监督音频数据和强制字符对齐的架构，成功解决了现代希伯来语G2P转换中因缺乏元音标注和发音口语化导致的难题，为希伯来语语音技术提供了更优的基准方案。

Abstract: Grapheme-to-phoneme (G2P) conversion for Modern Hebrew is needed for applications like text-to-speech (TTS), but is challenging due to the language's abjad writing system, which leaves vowels largely unwritten, creating substantial ambiguity. Standard approaches first predict vowel diacritics (nikud) to produce International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA) transcriptions, but this is limited: vocalization data is scarce and laborious to produce, it does not specify features such as lexical stress, and it reflects formal grammatical rules rather than everyday spoken pronunciation. Direct sequence-to-sequence IPA prediction, meanwhile, struggles on limited data and fails to exploit the character-level alignment characteristic of abjads. Our method, ReNikud, overcomes these limitations with two key insights: (1) Weak audio supervision via a phoneme-based automatic speech recognition (ASR) pseudo-labeling pipeline on thousands of hours of unlabeled Hebrew audio, yielding phonemic transcriptions that reflect natural spoken norms without manual annotation. (2) A pseudo-vocalization architecture that predicts IPA phonemes at each character position, enforcing character-level alignment as an inductive bias. Results on existing Hebrew G2P benchmarks and the new targeted MILIM benchmark for spoken Hebrew show that ReNikud surpasses previous state-of-the-art methods. We will release our code and trained models to support further work on Hebrew TTS and speech technologies.

### [48] [Pitch Spelling Jazz Lead Sheets, Solo Transcriptions, Classical Piano and Monophonic Scores](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20198)
*Augustin Bouquillard,Florent Jacquemard*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合两阶段优化（调式与调性）的算法，能从MIDI数据中准确识别音名、调号及局部调式，从而自动生成高质量的乐谱，适用于多种音乐风格的转录任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决音乐自动转录（特别是从音频转录的爵士乐）中存在的音高拼写（Pitch Spelling）和调性识别问题，旨在实现更高质量的乐谱自动生成，以便于音乐分析、教学及文化遗产保护。

Method: 该算法包含两个优化阶段：第一阶段为“调式”阶段，通过最短路径搜索为每个小节选择最可能的音阶，以最小化乐谱中的变音记号；第二阶段为“调性”阶段，基于局部音阶估计全局调号及准确的音名，从而实现全曲的最佳记谱效果。同时，作者定义了新的爵士音阶间距离度量。

Result: 该算法在多种类型的数字乐谱数据集上进行了验证，包括爵士乐谱（Real Book）、爵士独奏与贝斯线转录、传统曲调以及古典钢琴与单声部乐器作品，表现出了良好的适用性和记谱准确性。

Conclusion: 该算法通过联合优化音高拼写、调号和局部调式，能够有效地将MIDI数据转化为具有良好可读性的乐谱，为音乐转录、分析和教学提供了有力工具。研究定义的爵士音阶间新距离也为音乐学研究提供了潜在价值。

Abstract: We present an algorithm for pitch spelling and key estimation. Given an input in MIDI-like format, containing information on note pitches (expressed in semitones relative to the lowest reference note) and bar boundaries, it estimates the appropriate note names, a global Key Signature, and a local scale for each bar. This related information elements are evaluated jointly during two stages of optimisation. During an initial 'modal' stage, a probable scale is proposed for each bar, minimising the number of accidentals to be printed in the printed score with a shortest-path search. Then, during a second stage called 'tonal', these local scales are used to estimate the Key Signature and note names that would result in the best musical notation for the entire piece. We present evaluations conducted on datasets comprising a variety of digital musical scores: jazz lead sheets taken from the Real Book, transcriptions of recordings of jazz soli and bass lines, traditional tunes, as well as classical scores for piano and monophonic instruments. Our procedure was originally designed for use in music transcription, specifically for building digital collections of jazz solos transcribed from audio recordings, for the purposes of music analysis, teaching and the preservation of cultural heritage. This method should also prove useful for other tasks related to the processing of musical notation. Furthermore, to this end, we have defined new distances between various common jazz scales, which may be of some interest to musicological studies.

### [50] [Actionable Activation Directions for Detecting and Mitigating Emergent Misalignment Across Language Model Families](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20225)
*Abdul Rafay Syed*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究发现大模型微调导致的不安全代码偏见存在于模型内部特定的可操作激活方向中，通过干预该方向可有效提升安全性，但这种干预手段难以在不同架构模型间实现特异性迁移，因此模型审计应回归模型内部探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语言模型在不安全代码上微调后会出现涌现式的对齐失效（misalignment），且其内部机制尚不明确。研究者旨在探究这种失效是否对应于不同架构模型间共享的、可因果干预的激活空间方向，从而寻找更有效的模型安全性修正手段。

Method: 研究团队对四种指令微调模型（Qwen2.5-1.5B, Gemma-2-2B, Llama-3.2-1B, Ministral-3-3B）进行了相同的不安全代码微调，提取末层激活值并计算“均值差方向”（difference-in-means direction）。通过因果引导（causal steering）技术验证该方向对不安全代码生成的抑制效果，并使用岭回归（ridge regression）评估跨架构方向迁移的有效性及特异性。

Result: 研究发现，每个模型内部存在一个可实现99.6%分离度的“均值差方向”，通过因果引导减去该方向可将代码外溢（code spillover）现象显著降低21-51个百分点。然而，跨架构迁移实验表明，尽管方向迁移能产生行为抑制，但缺乏特异性（随机方向效果相当），且模型间呈现非对称的迁移拓扑关系（Gemma和Qwen作为几何供给方，Llama作为接收方）。

Conclusion: 该研究明确了跨架构线性修正的局限性，指出尽管模型内部存在可操作的“不安全代码”表征方向，但这种方向在模型间并不具备高度的特异性。因此，针对模型安全性的审计和对齐干预应优先采用“模型内探测”（within-model probing）方法，而非依赖通用的跨模型迁移。

Abstract: Fine-tuning language models on insecure code induces emergent misalignment with poorly understood internal structure. We investigate whether this misalignment corresponds to a causally actionable activation-space direction shared across architectures. Across four instruction-tuned model families (Qwen2.5-1.5B, Gemma-2-2B, Llama-3.2-1B, Ministral-3-3B) finetuned identically, a difference-in-means direction achieves 99.6% separation of aligned and misaligned activations at each model's final layer. Causal steering by subtracting this direction reduces code spillover by 21-51 points, while a secure-code control confirms content specificity. Cross-architecture transfer via ridge regression maps yields large behavioral suppression (up to 46 points) but fails specificity controls as random and orthogonal directions perform comparably. We identify a two-tier specificity structure: within-model directions are causally specific and actionable; cross-model directions are causally real but non-specific. An asymmetric transfer topology emerges, with Gemma and Qwen acting as geometric donors and Llama as a receiver. These findings define the limits of linear cross-architecture correction and recommend within-model probing for auditing.

### [51] [The Register Gap: A Meaning Intelligence Framework for Nigerian Public Discourse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20255)
*Celestine Achi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对尼日利亚话语体系中语境复杂性难以通过简单情感分类解决的问题，提出了包含九个维度的“意义智能框架”（MIF）。实验证明，通过提供该框架引导，大型语言模型在处理尼日利亚多语言变体的语境理解、潜台词识别及策略推荐能力上均有显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有尼日利亚语言情感分析基准（如NaijaSenti）仅关注三分类情感（正面、负面、中性），忽略了语境对交流意图的关键影响。AI系统在尼日利亚语境下的失败主要归因于“语境缺失”而非翻译错误，因此需要一套能够区分表层情感与真实意图的评估体系。

Method: 研究提出了包含九个维度的“意义智能框架”（MIF），涵盖语体、表层情感、真实意图、反讽、潜台词、风险等级、标注置信度、说话者情绪及推荐行动。研究构建了包含标准英语、尼日利亚英语、尼日利亚皮钦语及代码混合语的30项校准数据集，对比了Gemini 2.5 Flash模型在零样本（zero-shot）与模式引导（schema-informed）提示下的表现。

Result: 应用MIF模式引导提示后，模型表现大幅提升：语体识别准确率从33.3%跃升至73.3%（提升40个百分点）；整体意义智能评分（Meaning Intelligence Score）从73.2提高至78.6；在检测潜台词和策略性建议方面分别取得了10分和10.3分的显著进步。

Conclusion: 研究表明，现有的情感分析基准在处理尼日利亚复杂语境时存在局限性。引入MIF框架能够显著提升大型语言模型对尼日利亚多语言、多语境话语的理解深度与准确性，特别是在语体识别、隐晦潜台词检测和策略性建议方面效果显著。

Abstract: We introduce the Meaning Intelligence Framework (MIF), a nine-dimension annotation and evaluation schema for Nigerian public discourse that separates surface sentiment from true communicative intent. Existing benchmarks for Nigerian languages, including NaijaSenti and AfriSenti, treat sentiment classification as a three-way polarity task (positive, negative, neutral). We argue that the dominant failure mode of AI systems on Nigerian discourse is not translation failure but context failure: the same utterance carries opposite pragmatic force depending on speaker, audience, and situation. The MIF operationalises this insight across nine scored dimensions: register, surface sentiment, true intent, irony, coded subtext, risk tier, annotator confidence, speaker emotion, and recommended communications action. We construct a 30-item calibration dataset spanning Standard English, Nigerian English, Nigerian Pidgin, and code-mixed registers, and evaluate a frontier language model (Gemini 2.5 Flash) under zero-shot and schema-informed prompting conditions. The headline finding is the Register Gap: zero-shot register classification accuracy is 33.3%, rising to 73.3% (+40 points) when the model receives the MIF schema in-context. The composite Meaning Intelligence Score increases by 5.4 points (73.2 to 78.6) under schema-informed prompting, with the largest practical gains in register identification, coded-subtext detection (+10 points), and strategic action recommendation (+10.3 points). We release the framework specification, annotation guidelines, and the 30-item public calibration set to support reproducibility, while retaining a private holdout corpus for contamination-protected evaluation.

</details>


### [52] [PsyScore: A Psychometrically-Aware Framework for Trait-Adaptive Essay Scoring and ZPD-Scaffolded Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20287)
*Wei Xia,Jin Wu,Haoran Shi,Xiangyu Wang,Chanjin Zheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PsyScore 是一款结合心理测量学模型与大语言模型的自动化作文评估框架，通过共享潜在能力表征，实现了可解释的精准评分与基于学习者水平的自适应教学反馈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自动作文评分（AES）方法通常将评分与反馈割裂开来：神经网络评分模型缺乏可解释性，而大模型生成的反馈往往忽略了学习者的个体能力水平差异。因此，迫切需要一种既能提供可靠评估又能提供个性化教学反馈的集成方案。

Method: 提出 PsyScore 框架，包含三个核心模块：1. 特征自适应神经 IRT 评分器（结合分级部分信用模型 GPCM，实现评分的可解释性）；2. 最近发展区（ZPD）脚手架反馈生成器（根据诊断出的能力参数动态调整反馈策略）；3. 多视角反馈评估策略（利用配对偏好判断和学生修订模拟评估反馈质量）。

Result: 在 ASAP++ 数据集上的实验结果表明，PsyScore 不仅实现了具有竞争力的自动评分性能，还能够提供更符合教学逻辑、针对性更强的指导性反馈。

Conclusion: PsyScore 通过将心理测量学模型与大语言模型反馈生成相结合，成功弥合了自动作文评分（AES）中评分准确性与反馈指导性之间的鸿沟。该框架证明了基于共享潜在能力表征的多任务集成是提升教育评估系统的有效路径。

Abstract: Effective Automated Essay Scoring (AES) are expected to support both reliable assessment and actionable instructional feedback. However, existing approaches often treat scoring and feedback as separate components: neural scoring models provide limited interpretability, while Large Language Model (LLM)-based feedback is typically insensitive to learners proficiency levels. To address this fragmentation, this work proposes PsyScore, a psychometrically-aware framework that integrates diagnostic assessment with instructional scaffolding through a shared latent ability representation. PsyScore comprises three key modules: a Trait-Adaptive Neural IRT Scorer that incorporates the Graded Partial Credit Model (GPCM) into a neural architecture, enabling the precise estimation of student ability while maintaining psychometric interpretability, a ZPD-Scaffolded Feedback Generator, which conditions multi-agent feedback strategies on the diagnosed ability parameter to adapt instructional focus across different proficiency levels, and a Multi-Perspective Feedback Evaluation Strategy that assesses feedback quality via pairwise preference judgements and student revision simulations. Experiments on the ASAP++ dataset demonstrate that PsyScore achieves competitive scoring performance while providing more pedagogically aligned feedback.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Online hate speech and misinformation frequently overlap, yet NLP research has mainly treated them in isolation. While LLMs represent a scalable solution for assisting humans in the generation of counterspeech for both threats, zero-shot models frequently generate repetitive and vague responses, underscoring the need for high-quality examples to steer model generation. However, existing counterspeech datasets against the overlap of hate and misinformation are scarce and limited to single-turn English dialogues, while real-life interactions span across multiple turns and languages. To bridge this gap, we introduce the first large-scale, expert-curated, multilingual dataset of dialogues tackling the intersection of hate and misinformation. To ensure factual grounding, the dialogues are also anchored in verified external knowledge (i.e., fact-checking articles and NGO reports) and include document- and chunk-level span annotations, making it directly applicable for RAG systems. ### [54] [Your Mouse and Eyes Secretly Leak Your Preference: LLM Alignment using Implicit Feedback from Users](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20482)
*Haw-Shiuan Chang,Jeffrey Gomez,Mehul Patwari,Aryan Sajith,Hamed Zamani*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型对齐方法高度依赖昂贵且稀缺的显式人类反馈，且未能利用互联网领域中已被证明极具价值的隐式反馈信息。

Method: 构建了一个名为IFLLM的新数据集，记录了59名用户在处理1336个多轮对话时的鼠标轨迹和眼动数据；开发了一种基于隐式用户反馈的奖励模型，并将该模型应用于DPO（直接偏好优化）算法中对八种大语言模型进行微调。

Result: 基于隐式反馈的奖励模型将偏好预测准确率从55%提升至64%；在对八种大语言模型应用DPO后，模型回复质量的相对提升幅度接近原来的三倍。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了隐式反馈（鼠标轨迹和眼动数据）在对齐大语言模型中的巨大潜力，能够有效弥补显式反馈数据稀缺的短板，显著提升模型对齐效果。

Abstract: To align a Large Language Model (LLM), most existing methods collect explicit human feedback and train a reward model to predict the human preference based on the response text. These existing methods have two key limitations. First, the users rarely provide explicit feedback for LLM responses, which makes the high-quality preference annotation expensive to collect. Second, the methods do not leverage implicit human feedback, which has proven vital to the economic moats of Internet giants. To quantify the value of implicit feedback, we build a new dataset called IFLLM, which collects 1336 multi-turn questions from the 59 Mechanical Turk workers, their mouse trajectories, and eye gazing points to the LLMs' responses from their webcams. IFLLM shows that the users have very diverse types of gazing behavior and mouse trajectories. Our reward model based on the implicit user feedback boosts the accuracy of the text-based reward model from 55% to 64% and nearly triples the relative response quality improvements after applying the DPO to eight LLMs, demonstrating the value of implicit feedback in the wild. Our data collection website, dataset, and codes can be found at https://github.com/themehulpatwari/llm-implicit-feedback/.

### [55] [Beyond Global Replanning: Hierarchical Recovery for Cross-Device Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20487)
*Shu Yao,Yuhua Luo,Qian Long,Jingru Fan,Zhuoyuan Yu,Yuheng Wang,Lin Wu,Yufan Dang,Huatao Li,Chen Qian*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 H-RePlan，一种用于多设备智能体的分层重规划框架。通过将设备局部故障处理与全局规划分离，该系统能更智能地应对跨设备任务中的动态故障，在提高任务成功率的同时降低了计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多设备智能体在面对任务执行失败时，缺乏对故障层级的精准识别。通常采用粗粒度的重试或全局重新规划，无法区分哪些问题可以在当前设备内自行解决，从而导致效率低下且应对能力受限。

Method: 提出了 H-RePlan 框架，该框架采用统一的 API-CLI-GUI 执行机制，并引入了“跨层故障抽象”技术，允许智能体在设备内部切换多种执行策略进行恢复，仅在局部无法解决时才触发上层的全局重新规划。同时开发了包含故障注入机制的 HeraBench 基准测试集。

Result: 实验结果表明，H-RePlan 在任务完成率、指令遵循度以及完美通过率上均显著优于现有的单策略及粗粒度多设备基准模型，同时在保证执行可靠性的前提下，显著降低了 token 消耗成本。

Conclusion: 分层级的恢复策略对于构建稳健的多设备智能体至关重要。通过将设备内的局部故障恢复与全局编排区分开，H-RePlan 有效提升了复杂任务执行的成功率并降低了资源消耗。

Abstract: Real-world computer-use tasks often span multiple applications and devices, requiring agents to coordinate heterogeneous environments under dynamic runtime failures. Existing multi-device agent systems support task decomposition and cross-device assignment, but recovery remains largely coarse-grained: when execution fails, they typically retry the same strategy, reassign the subtask, or revise the global plan, without systematically modeling the device-local strategy space. This limits their ability to distinguish failures that can be repaired within the current device from those that require cross-device replanning. We propose \textbf{H-RePlan}, a hierarchical replanning framework for multi-device agents with unified API--CLI--GUI execution. H-RePlan equips each device with interchangeable execution strategies and separates device-local strategy recovery from orchestrator-level global replanning through a compact cross-layer failure abstraction. To evaluate this capability, we introduce \textbf{HeraBench}, a fault-injected benchmark that constructs cross-device workflows over Linux and Android devices and injects strategy- and device-level failures. Experiments show that H-RePlan substantially outperforms single-strategy and coarse-grained multi-device baselines, achieving higher completion, instruction adherence, and perfect-pass rates while reducing the token cost required for reliable end-to-end success. These results demonstrate that scope-aware hierarchical recovery is essential for robust multi-device agent execution.

</details>


### [56] [StylisticBias: A Few Human Visual Cues Drive Most Social Biases in MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20527)
*Shaghayegh Kolli,Timo Cavelius,Nafiseh Nikeghbal,Samantha Dalal,Jana Diesner*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究推出了StylisticBias基准，通过控制变量法系统性量化了多模态大模型在社会判断中的视觉偏见，发现模型对少数特定外观属性存在显著偏差，为模型公平性评估提供了新工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在社会关键领域应用日益广泛，但目前关于视觉线索如何影响模型对人的评价尚缺乏深入研究。现有工作多对比不同群体，难以区分“身份差异”与“视觉外观属性”对偏见的影响，因此需要一个更精确的基准来解耦这些变量。

Method: 研究者构建了名为“StylisticBias”的受控评估基准。他们生成了500张基础人脸图像，并为每张人脸创建了约50种单属性变体（总计约2.5万张图片），通过固定身份的同时仅改变单个视觉属性的方法，精确测量特定视觉线索如何影响模型的社会判断。研究在6个多模态大模型（MLLMs）上测试了25个二元社会判断场景。

Result: 实验发现：1. 年龄和体型对身份层面的判断影响最大；2. 时尚风格等视觉线索导致了属性层面的最大偏移；3. 约15种特定属性导致了模型80%的偏见变异；4. 当判断任务与外观在语义上相关（如社会经济地位、时尚风格）时，模型的敏感度最高。

Conclusion: StylisticBias提供了一个有效的基准，能够细致地量化MLLMs在社会判断中的偏见来源。研究强调了模型对特定视觉属性（尤其是年龄、体型和时尚风格）的高度敏感性，并指出社会偏见并非均匀分布，而是集中在少数几个关键的视觉维度上，这为未来构建更公平的AI模型提供了明确的改进方向。

Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are increasingly deployed in personally and societally consequential settings, yet the visual cues that shape how these models judge people remain poorly understood. Prior work often compares different (groups of) individuals, making it difficult to separate appearance effects from identity differences. We introduce StylisticBias, a controlled benchmark for evaluating attribute-level social bias in MLLMs. We generate 500 photorealistic base faces and create about 50 single-attribute variations per face, producing about 25K images. This design keeps identity fixed and changes one visual attribute at a time. It lets us measure how specific cues shift model judgments. We evaluate six MLLMs across 25 binary social judgment scenarios. We find that age and body type dominate identity-level effects, while fashion style and other visual cues drive the largest attribute-level shifts. We further find that about 15 attributes account for nearly 80\% of the total variation, showing that bias is concentrated in a small set of visual cues. Sensitivity is strongest in judgments that are semantically aligned with appearance, especially socioeconomic and style-related judgments. We release StylisticBias as a benchmark for fine-grained bias evaluation in multimodal models. Code and dataset: https://github.com/timo-cavelius/StylisticBias and https://hf.co/datasets/shaghayegh/stylistic-bias-dataset.

</details>

### [57] [Computational Identifiability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19361)
*Lucius E. J. Bynum,Rajesh Ranganath,Kyunghyun Cho*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“计算可识别性”新框架，旨在取代传统的理想化理论可识别性。该方法通过有限的计算搜索程序来判断因果效应是否在特定约束下可被估计，从而更好地解决现实中复杂、有限样本及混合数据环境下的因果推断挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的因果可识别性通常假设无限数据或理想化的数学条件（理论可识别性），这在面对现实中有限样本、模糊图形标准、观测与干预混合数据以及复杂反事实推理时往往显得力不从心。研究者旨在弥合理想化数学模型与实际应用场景之间的差距，探索一种由计算约束定义的新型可识别性框架。

Method: 本文提出了一种“计算可识别性（computational identifiability）”框架。该方法不再单纯依赖于渐近性质或理想化的数学条件，而是定义了一个有限的计算搜索过程（computational search procedure）来寻找满足特定误差容限的经验估计器。该过程受限于指定的先验分布和具体的搜索算法，通过实证评估来判断因果查询是否在计算层面上可被识别。

Result: 实验结果表明，该框架能够有效地解决多种细粒度、实际的因果识别问题，包括：在有限样本下的识别、在模糊图形标准下的识别、混合观测与干预数据的处理，以及跨反事实数据的估算。通过将可识别性与计算过程挂钩，该方法在实际应用场景中表现出更强的实用性和适应性。

Conclusion: 传统的理论可识别性在处理现实世界的有限数据、复杂混合数据及不确定性条件时存在局限。本文提出的“计算可识别性”框架将可识别性转化为一个有限的计算搜索过程，通过将估计器的存在性与具体的计算流程绑定，为因果推断提供了一种更务实、更具灵活性且适用于实际操作的评估方法。

Abstract: Identification conditions describe the computability of a target query or parameter of interest as a function of the type and amount of information available. In causal identification, this information is often expressed in the form of a causal graph, and data are observed or collected for some subset of variables in the graph. Target queries may be for a single effect alone or for a class of effects in a given model. The derivation of an identification algorithm then defines mathematically the process by which the desired causal effect(s) can be uniquely determined, theoretically, in expectation. Identifiability in expectation, or 'theoretical identifiability,' generally assumes asymptotic properties, infinite data, or other mathematically idealized conditions. In this paper, we explore a fundamental distinction between this theoretical, idealized notion of identifiability and a proposed alternative that is computation-bound. The framework we propose - 'computational identifiability' - is to instead define a finite computational search procedure for an empirical estimator. If this process finds an estimator empirically, within a desired error tolerance, then identifiability is satisfied, conditional on the specified assumptions of the search (i.e., a prior distribution over the parameters) and conditional on the search procedure itself. Through several experiments, we demonstrate how this framework allows us to answer fine-grained, practical identification questions, such as identification with small finite samples, with ambiguous graphical criteria, with mixed observational-interventional data, and across counterfactual data and estimands. Code is available at https://github.com/lbynum/metadentify.

</details>


### [58] [When to Trust, How to Distill: Multi-Foundation Model Guidance for Lightweight, Robust Scientific Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19363)
*Rupasree Dey,Abdul Matin,Nathan Orwick,Yao Zhang,Shrideep Pallickara,Sangmi Lee Pallickara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决基础模型在科学领域应用中的分布偏移和高计算成本问题，Guard框架通过动态路由和不确定性门控机制，从多个基础模型中蒸馏知识，从而训练出适合边缘设备的高效、高精度专业预测模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间序列基础模型（TSFMs）虽具备通用时序动态编码能力，但面临领域分布偏移问题导致零样本性能不佳，且计算成本过高，难以在资源受限的边缘计算传感器网络中部署。本研究旨在探索如何从这些不匹配的基础模型中提取结构化知识，以训练轻量级的专业预测模型。

Method: 提出了Guard（Gated Uncertainty-Aware Routing for Distillation）框架，包含两个核心机制：1. 上下文路由器（Contextual Router）：根据输入数据的局部统计特征，动态选择最相关的教师模型；2. 不确定性门控温度机制（Uncertainty-Gated Temperature）：当教师模型的不确定性较高时，自动降低其蒸馏权重，防止误导。

Result: 在气象、生态碳通量、土壤湿度和能源电网四个气候关键领域进行了评估，Guard框架显著降低了均方根误差（RMSE），并证明即便教师模型本身在特定领域性能欠佳，仍能在28.5%的最难预测样本中提供关键纠正作用，优于全球最优的基础模型。

Conclusion: Guard框架证明了即使在分布偏移的情况下，利用多教师模型进行选择性知识蒸馏，可以有效克服时间序列基础模型在特定科学领域的局限性，并为资源受限的边缘计算环境提供了一种高精度、轻量级的预测解决方案。

Abstract: The deployment of Time-Series Foundation Models (TSFMs) in physical sciences is hindered by a critical trade-off: while these models encode rich, universal temporal dynamics, they suffer from severe distributional misalignment when applied zero-shot to specific scientific domains, and their computational cost prohibits deployment in edge-computing sensor networks. We address a fundamental challenge: How can we extract latent structural knowledge from misaligned foundation models (FM) to train lightweight, specialized forecasters? We propose Gated Uncertainty-Aware Routing for Distillation (Guard), a novel framework that reframes multiteacher distillation as an instance-wise decision process with two adaptive mechanisms: (1) a Contextual Router that dynamically selects the most relevant teacher based on local input statistics, exploiting complementarity across diverse foundation models; and (2) an Uncertainty-Gated Temperature mechanism that acts as a "circuit-breaker," automatically attenuating distillation strength when teacher confidence diverges from domain reality. We evaluate our proposed lightweight framework on four climate-critical domains: meteorology, ecosystem carbon flux, soil moisture, and energy grids. Our method significantly reduces RMSE relative to a fixed-weight multi-teacher distillation baseline, successfully distilling knowledge from pretrained FMs (teachers) even when they exhibit suboptimal zero-shot accuracy due to distribution shift between the original and target data domains. We demonstrate that these domain-misaligned teachers can still serve as critical correctives, outperforming the globally superior FMs on 28.5% of the hardest instances. Ultimately, this enables high-precision scientific forecasting suitable for resource-constrained edge deployment. Code is available at https://github.com/RupasreeDey/GUARD-KDD2026.

</details>


### [59] [Closing the Social-Semantic Gap: SPSD for Edge-Based Prompt Compression in Cloud LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19364)
*Abhinit Sen,Ajeet Kumar,Manaranjan Pradhan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文提出了 SPSD 架构，通过边缘侧小模型过滤提示词中的冗余社交用语，在保证大模型回复质量的前提下，有效减少了输入 Token 数量，从而显著降低云端推理成本与能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型推理中的 Prefill（预填充）阶段能耗巨大。研究发现，用户输入的提示词中包含大量如客套话、道歉前言等“社会脚手架”内容，这些内容对机器推理的边际信息增益极低，导致了“社会-语义鸿沟”，作者旨在通过压缩这些冗余信息来降低云端推理成本。

Method: 提出 SPSD（情感保留语义蒸馏）流程：利用边缘侧轻量化模型（如 4-bit 量化的 Gemma-2-2B-Instruct）对用户提示词进行压缩，去除其中低信息量的社交修辞（即“社会-语义鸿沟”部分），再将精简后的提示词发送至云端大模型；同时采用基于规则的门控机制，确保安全敏感领域的提示词不被处理。

Result: 实验表明，SPSD 平均每次调用可节省 99.9 个输入 Token，且所有样本均有节约；在响应质量评估中，蒸馏后的提示词与原始提示词相比表现出非劣性，甚至在 28% 的情况下更优；估算单次调用可节省 70-270 uWh 的净能耗。

Conclusion: SPSD 证明了在边缘端进行提示词蒸馏是一种有效且实用的策略，能够在保持回复质量非劣性的前提下，显著降低云端大模型的输入 Token 消耗和计算能耗，为缓解推理成本压力提供了新思路。

Abstract: The prefill stage of Large Language Model (LLM) inference is a growing contributor to cloud-scale energy cost. Many consumer-support and conversational prompts contain social scaffolding: politeness markers, apologetic preamble, repetition, and rapport-building language that is important for human communication but carries low marginal information for machine reasoning. We call this discrepancy the Social-Semantic Gap. We present SPSD (Sentiment Preserving Semantic Distillation), an edge-based pipeline that compresses user prompts using a 4-bit quantised Small Language Model before transmission to a cloud-deployed LLM. Evaluation on a 248-prompt corpus using Gemma-2-2B-Instruct (Q4_K_M) as the SLM and Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct as the cloud evaluation model yields a mean input token saving of 99.9 tokens per distilled call, with all 146 distilled calls yielding positive savings. Response quality, assessed by blind LLM-as-judge scoring across 121 pairs, is non-inferior to the raw path within a pre-specified 1-point margin on a 15-point rubric; the judge awarded 43 percent ties, 28 percent distilled wins, and 29 percent raw wins. Cosine similarity is mixed: mean 0.682, median 0.712, with 54.1 percent of pairs above the 0.70 reference threshold. Safety-critical domains are conservatively routed to passthrough via rule-based gates. Per-call net energy saving is estimated at 70-270 uWh under stated assumptions. SPSD shows that on-device prompt distillation can reduce cloud LLM input-token cost while preserving response quality within a practical non-inferiority margin.

</details>


### [60] [Performance Analysis and Optimization of 3D Generative Diffusion Models across GPU Architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19365)
*Jeeho Ryoo,Yongchan Jung,Muhammad Ali Khaliq,Weidong Zhang,Jiatong Han,Byeong Kil Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了医学3D扩散模型在GPU上的性能瓶颈，通过架构感知优化（TF32和通道最后布局），在不损失精度的前提下，实现了算力效率的大幅提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管扩散模型在3D MRI合成领域表现出色，但其部署因极高的GPU算力需求（多次U-Net迭代）及高度异构的内核行为而受到严重限制，亟需通过底层架构分析来识别并消除性能瓶颈。

Method: 本文对Med-DDPM在三代NVIDIA GPU架构上进行了深度性能剖析，涵盖内核级运行时分解、指令混合特性、内存系统利用率、Warp活动及分析器优先级评分。在此基础上，应用了TF32 Tensor Core激活和3D通道最后（channels-last）内存布局优化。

Result: 优化方案在A100架构上取得了显著成效：SM周期减少至1/100，动态指令减少至1/100，Tensor Core利用率提升至原来的近10倍（1.45倍至9.98倍），IPC提升了7%，且模型合成质量未受影响。

Conclusion: 通过针对性的架构感知优化（TF32 Tensor Core激活和3D通道最后布局），研究证明了可以在保持生成质量的前提下，显著提升Med-DDPM在GPU上的运行效率，为医学图像扩散模型的高效部署提供了关键技术路径。

Abstract: Diffusion models have become essential for high-fidelity 3D MRI synthesis, yet their deployment remains constrained by substantial GPU resource demands arising from hundreds of U-Net evaluations per sample and a highly heterogeneous kernel behavior. This paper performs a comprehensive performance analysis of the state-of-the-art medical diffusion model, Med-DDPM, across three generations of NVIDIA architectures to study kernel-level runtime breakdowns, instruction-mix characteristics, memory system utilization, warp-level activities, and profiler priority-score estimates. We show that training is overwhelmingly dominated by cuDNN convolution and implicit-GEMM kernels, with inefficiencies arising from memory-access patterns, tensor-layout conversions, and limited Tensor Core utilization. Guided by these insights, we evaluate two architecture-aware optimizations TF32 Tensor Core activation and a 3D channels-last layout and demonstrate that they reduce SM cycles by up to 100x, cut dynamic instructions by 100x, raise Tensor Core utilization from 1.45 to 9.98x, and increase IPC by 7% on A100, all without degrading synthesis quality.

### [61] [Information Lattice Learning as Probabilistic Graphical Model Structure Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19366)
*Haizi Yu,Lav R. Varshney*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将信息格学习（ILL）与概率图模型（PGM）结合，证明 ILL 实际上是一种针对商变量的可解释约束因子图的结构学习方法，连接了符号规则提取与最大熵概率建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管信息格学习（ILL）在提取信号的可解释规则方面表现优异，但其在处理概率质量函数时，与统计学中成熟的概率图模型（PGM）之间的理论关系尚不明确。本文旨在通过概率图模型框架重新诠释 ILL，以揭示其在统计建模中的本质特征。

Method: 该研究通过将 ILL 的规则与概率图模型（PGM）建立映射，提出将分区视为诱导出的确定性商变量，并将规则定义为该变量的边际定律。研究对比了通用提升（满足约束的可行联合分布）与特殊提升（基于 L2 一致性原理或香农熵的最大熵重构），并指出在香农熵下，ILL 学习出的规则等价于对数线性因子图。

Result: 研究证明了 ILL 学习到的规则对应于基于可解释抽象的边际约束；明确了信息格本身的边际约束结构（非贝叶斯网络）；验证了 ILL 的重构过程与最大熵原理的紧密联系，并成功将其建模为基于商变量的约束因子图。

Conclusion: 信息格学习（ILL）本质上是关于商变量的可解释约束因子图的结构学习方法。该视角清晰地阐明了 ILL 与图形模型及最大熵模型的内在联系，并为未来在推理、可辨识性及符号-概率混合学习领域的研究提供了新的理论方向。

Abstract: Information lattice learning (ILL) learns interpretable rules of a signal by alternately projecting the signal onto a partition lattice that encodes a hierarchy of abstractions and lifting selected rules back to the signal domain. When the signal is a probability mass function, we show the probabilistic rules learned by ILL admit a natural probabilistic graphical model (PGM) interpretation and develop this interpretation in detail. A partition in ILL induces a deterministic quotient variable, and a rule is the marginal law of that quotient variable. A rule set is therefore a collection of marginal constraints over interpretable abstractions. General lifting is the feasible family of all joint distributions satisfying those constraints, while special lifting chooses a maximum-ignorance reconstruction, implemented in ILL by an L2 uniformity principle closely related to maximum entropy. Under a Shannon-entropy lifting, the same constraints yield a log-linear factor graph whose factors are indexed by learned abstractions. The information lattice itself, however, is not a Bayesian network: its edges encode refinement and coarsening of abstractions, not conditional dependence. Thus ILL is best viewed as structure learning for interpretable constraint-based factor graphs over quotient variables. This view clarifies how ILL relates to graphical models and maximum entropy models, while suggesting new directions for inference, identifiability, and hybrid symbolic-probabilistic learning.

### [62] [Weibull Weight-Scale Parameter Evolution under AdamW Training Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19367)
*Tiexin Ding*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文解析了 AdamW 训练中权重规模参数 $\lambda$ 的动力学行为，通过推导“三力分解”模型证实了对齐力是权重增长的主驱动力，并提出了一种高效的样条位移方法来监控这些训练动态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示 AdamW 优化器训练过程中权重规模参数 $\lambda$ 呈现“增长—过冲—放松”这一特殊演变模式背后的物理机制，并探索如何通过有限的训练数据恢复这些潜在的动力学过程。

Method: 1. 基于双参数 Weibull 分布框架分析 Transformer 权重分布。
2. 推导了 AdamW 更新中平方权重范数的“三力分解”模型（对齐力、注入力、衰减力）。
3. 使用 Pythia-70M 模型进行实证研究，验证各力对权重增长的贡献。
4. 提出了一种“样条位移方法”（Spline Displacement Method），用于在缺乏优化器矩信息的实际场景中，从稀疏检查点重建对齐力。

Result: 1. 对齐力在训练的上升阶段占主导地位，贡献了 88-94% 的绝对力预算，且对超级权重（super-weights）的去除具有鲁棒性。
2. 权重饱和过程是由对齐力和衰减力达到平衡所导致的。
3. 样条位移方法能以 92-94% 的准确率从稀疏检查点还原对齐力，优于基准方法。
4. $\lambda(t)$ 的峰值与训练数据的相干性有关，暗示了权重缩放存在数据依赖性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，AdamW 训练过程中权重规模参数 $\lambda$ 的演变是由对齐力（Alignment）、注入力（Injection）和衰减力（Decay）这三种力的动态平衡所驱动的。对齐力是推动权重增长的核心因素，而衰减力在权重达到饱和时起到平衡作用。此外，样条位移方法可有效从稀疏检查点还原这些动力学特征。

Abstract: Building on a two-parameter Weibull framework for diagnosing transformer weight distributions, we study why the Weibull weight-scale parameter $λ$ grows, overshoots, and then relaxes during AdamW training. We derive a leading-order three-force decomposition of the squared weight norm from the AdamW update: an alignment force measuring the correlation between weights and the adaptive update direction, an injection force from adaptive step magnitude, and a decay force from decoupled weight decay. On self-trained Pythia-70M models with ground-truth optimizer moments, alignment dominates the rise phase, contributing 88-94% of the absolute force budget across four random seeds and remaining robust to super-weight removal. Near saturation, alignment and decay approach balance, explaining the transition from weight-scale growth to relaxation. These force dynamics directly govern the squared-norm component underlying $λ(t)$; the remaining RMS-to-Weibull reconstruction offset is measurable and decomposes into bridge and integration components, totaling approximately 5-6% in densely sampled regions. To extend the analysis to real models where optimizer moments are unavailable, we introduce a spline displacement method that recovers the alignment force from sparse checkpoints with approximately 92-94% accuracy, about twice the naive two-point baseline. We further observe that the peak value of $λ(t)$ varies with training-data coherence in our experiments, suggesting a data-dependent component of weight-scale growth that we leave to a controlled follow-up study. Code and data are available at https://github.com/tiexinding/NPM-Weibull-public.

</details>


### [63] [Zero-Inflated Gaussian Distributions Enable Parameter-Space Sparsity in Estimation-of-Distribution Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19369)
*Andreas Faust,Sven Nitzsche,Juergen Becker*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对稀疏黑盒优化问题，本文提出了一种基于零膨胀高斯分布的分布估计算法（ZIG-EDA），实现了稀疏模式与参数值的联合自动化优化，无需手工设计稀疏算子即可达到优异的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的分布估计算法（EDA）在连续空间中表现良好，但在稀疏优化问题上缺乏有效的通用机制。现有的稀疏优化方法往往依赖于手工设计的算子或复杂的双层方案，违背了EDA设计初衷，且引入了人为偏见。因此，研究旨在开发一种无需特定算子设计的通用稀疏EDA方法。

Method: 提出了多变量零膨胀高斯（ZIG）分布作为EDA的采样定律。通过潜在高斯模型，利用独立的指示维度和数值维度来表示稀疏模式、激活参数间的相关性以及两者间的交互。同时，引入了基于摊销反演（amortized inversion-based）的参数估计器，实现了对潜在参数的高效识别。

Result: 在Lunar Lander基准测试中，ZIG-EDA算法在收敛速度和最终优化结果上均优于稠密高斯EDA、手工设计的稀疏进化算法及其他临时稀疏EDA方法，且能够有效发现仅含少量活跃参数的高效控制器。

Conclusion: 本研究成功地将零膨胀高斯（ZIG）分布引入分布估计算法（EDA）框架，证明了在稀疏黑盒优化中，可以通过概率建模的方式实现稀疏模式与参数值的联合优化，克服了传统方法依赖手工设计稀疏算子的缺陷。

Abstract: Estimation-of-distribution algorithms (EDAs) are a powerful class of evolutionary methods for black-box optimization, especially when little is known about the structure of the objective. Whereas classical evolutionary algorithms rely on hand-designed mutation and crossover operators, hard to devise for unknown problem structures, and a source of bias, EDAs sidestep operator design entirely: they fit a probability distribution to the best individuals and sample the next generation from it. EDAs are well established on continuous parameter spaces, but they have not previously been generalized to sparse ones, in which most coefficients of a good solution are exactly zero. Existing sparse black-box optimizers therefore reintroduce exactly what EDAs were designed to avoid: hand-crafted sparsity operators, bi-level schemes alternating between support set and active values, zeroing thresholds, and other baked-in assumptions. We close this gap by proposing multivariate zero-inflated Gaussian (ZIG) distributions as EDA sampling laws. A latent Gaussian model with separate indicator and value dimensions represents sparsity patterns, correlations among active parameters, and the interactions between the two, so sparsity patterns and active values are optimized jointly, hierarchy-free. We show that the latent parameters of this model are identifiable from observed samples, unlike in the missing-data settings where related constructions originate, and introduce practical amortized inversion-based estimators for them. The estimators accurately recover latent correlation structures, and on the Lunar Lander benchmark the resulting ZIG-EDA converges faster and reaches higher final returns than a dense Gaussian EDA, a hand-crafted sparse evolutionary algorithm, and an ad-hoc sparse EDA, while finding controllers with only a small fraction of parameters active.

### [64] [Human-like autonomy emerges from self-play and a pinch of human data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19370)
*Daphne Cornelisse,Julian Hunt,Zixu Zhang,Waël Doulazmi,Kevin Joseph,Jaime Fernández Fisac,Eugene Vinitsky*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过在自我对弈强化学习中引入少量（30分钟）人类演示作为正则化手段，以极低的成本和训练开销，解决了自动驾驶策略与人类行为不兼容的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了一种将极少量（约30分钟）人类演示数据作为正则化目标引入自我对弈强化学习的方法。该方法在以最小化安全目标达成奖励为主体的基础上，利用这些少量的人类数据引导策略学习符合人类驾驶习惯的行为，从而避免了传统方法中复杂的奖励工程或大规模域随机化。

Result: 该方法仅需30分钟人类演示数据（比同类模仿学习少2500倍），在单块消费级显卡上仅需15小时即可完成训练。实验结果表明，训练出的策略能够有效地与未见过的人类轨迹进行协作，且具备良好的可扩展性和实用性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，通过将少量人类演示数据作为一种正则化手段引入自我对弈强化学习框架，可以有效解决纯自我对弈导致的驾驶行为非人性化问题。这种“以点带面”的策略极大地降低了对人类数据的依赖，且训练效率极高，为自动驾驶策略的训练提供了一种更具扩展性和实用性的方案。

Abstract: Self-play reinforcement learning has recently emerged as a way to train driving policies without any human data. It uses cheap, large-scale simulations to substitute expensive, large-scale human driving demonstrations. A key limitation of this approach is that policies trained through pure self-play can learn effective but alien driving conventions incompatible with people. Previous works attempt to mitigate such behavioral misalignments through extensive reward engineering and domain randomization, which are brittle and labor-intensive. Instead of completely discarding human demonstrations, our method treats them as a regularization objective on top of a minimal safe goal-reaching reward. Like the spice in a good stew, we find that a little human data goes a long way: our method uses only 30 minutes of human demonstrations, 2500x fewer than comparable imitation learning approaches. Resulting policies coordinate with held-out human trajectories and complete training in 15 hours on a single consumer-grade GPU. Videos and full source code are available at https://spiced-self-play.com/.

### [65] [ProMUSE: Progressive Multi-modal Uncertainty-guided Staged Evidential Alzheimer Disease Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19371)
*Long Doan,Branden Chen,Ethan Litton,Huan Huang,Jiajing Huang,Yixin Xie,Weihua Zhou,Nandakumar Narayanan,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ProMUSE 是一种能够按需调用高成本影像数据（MRI/PET）的阿尔茨海默病诊断框架，通过引入不确定性引导机制，在大幅降低诊断成本的同时维持了高水平的预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阿尔茨海默病的早期诊断至关重要，但传统的全模态（临床评估+MRI+PET）诊断方案成本高昂且难以普及，导致在实际临床流程中难以实现全面应用。因此，需要一种既能保持准确度又能降低高成本成像模态依赖的诊断策略。

Method: 提出了名为 ProMUSE 的渐进式多模态不确定性引导阶段性证据网络。该方法采用阶梯式诊断策略：首先利用低成本的临床数据进行初步的证据分类，并利用基于狄利克雷分布的主观逻辑模型量化不确定性；当不确定性超过预设阈值时，系统才会动态引入高成本的 MRI 或 PET 数据；最后通过登普斯特-沙夫尔理论（Dempster-Shafer theory）融合各模态的信念与不确定性，实现校准后的多模态预测。

Result: 在 ADNI、AIBL 和 OASIS 数据集上的实验结果表明，ProMUSE 在 CN-AD、CN-MCI 和 MCI-AD 等多种任务中，在减少 50%-90% 的 MRI/PET 使用率的前提下，达到了与全模态基线模型相当甚至更优的诊断准确率，实现了显著的成本节约。

Conclusion: ProMUSE 是一种实用、具有不确定性感知且资源高效的阿尔茨海默病辅助诊断方案，能够通过按需获取模态数据显著降低临床诊断成本，同时保持与全模态方法相当甚至更优的诊断准确率，具有极高的临床应用潜力。

Abstract: Alzheimer's disease (AD) is a fatal disorder that destroys memory and cognitive skills in the elderly population. Most treatments for AD are effective in the early stage, leading to an increasing demand for early AD diagnosis. AD diagnosis increasingly relies on multimodal data such as clinical assessments, structural Magnetic Resonance Imaging (MRI), and Positron Emission Tomography (PET) imaging. However, MRI and PET acquisition remain costly and not universally accessible, making full-modality inference impractical in real-world clinical workflows. We propose ProMUSE, a Progressive Multi-modal Uncertainty Guided Staged Evidential Network that adaptively determines when additional modalities are necessary, helping reduce the overall cost of data acquisition while maintaining accuracy. ProMUSE first performs evidential classification using low-cost clinical data and quantifies uncertainty via a Dirichlet-based subjective logic model. When uncertainty exceeds a learned threshold, ProMUSE progressively incorporates MRI or PET features, fusing modality-wise belief and uncertainty through Dempster-Shafer theory to obtain a calibrated multimodal prediction. This staged acquisition strategy enables accurate diagnosis while minimizing reliance on expensive imaging. Experiments on ADNI, AIBL, and OASIS across CN-AD, CN-MCI, and MCI-AD tasks demonstrate that ProMUSE achieves competitive or superior accuracy compared to full-modality baselines while reducing MRI/PET usage by 50-90%, yielding substantial cost savings. These results highlight ProMUSE as a practical, uncertainty-aware, and resource-efficient solution for real-world AD screening.

### [66] [cAPM: Continual AI-Assisted Pace-Mapping with Active Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19373)
*Dylan O'Hara,Pradeep Bajracharya,Casey Meisenzahl,Karli Gillette,Anton J. Prassl,Gernot Plank,Saman Nazarian,Roderick Tung,John L Sapp,Linwei Wang*

TL;DR: 针对 VT 消融中的起搏映射效率问题，本文提出 cAPM 框架，通过引入持续学习和主动学习策略，能够跨任务积累经验，大幅减少定位所需的起搏次数，显著提升手术效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床 VT 起搏映射效率低下，且现有AI方法缺乏跨患者或跨任务的知识迁移能力，无法有效减少手术中所需的起搏点数量，亟需一种能够持续学习并优化映射过程的智能方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为 cAPM 的持续AI辅助起搏映射框架。该框架由三个核心部分组成：1. 一个任务无关的代理神经网络，用于学习从起搏位点到12导联心电图形态的映射；2. 主动学习策略，用于选择最具信息量的下一个起搏位点；3. 持续学习策略，在处理多个目标时积累并保留先验知识，无需对每个新任务进行重训练。

Result: 在模拟测试中，cAPM 在使用 4.5 个起搏点的情况下，实现了 81% 的定位准确率（5mm容差内），而现有最优主动学习方法在使用 13.7 个起搏点时仅达到 38% 的准确率，性能优势显著。

Conclusion: cAPM 框架通过持续学习策略有效地跨任务迁移心脏起搏定位知识，显著提升了心室心动过速（VT）消融手术中定位的效率和精度，具备了向临床转化应用的基础。

Abstract: Ventricular tachycardia is a life-threatening rhythm disorder and a major cause of sudden cardiac death. Pace-mapping is a clinical procedure for identifying the intervention target during catheter ablation of VT. It requires clinicians to pace different sites in the ventricles and rapidly interpret the resulting electrocardiograms to determine where to pace next or whether a target site has been identified. Active learning AI models have been proposed to guide clinicians to the next pacing site, showing promise in reducing the number of pacing sites and improving the efficiency of pace-mapping. Existing methods require retraining each target without the ability to transfer knowledge across multiple VTs within the same patient or across patients. We introduce cAPM for continuous AI-assisted pace-mapping to capture and transfer knowledge accumulated from past pace-mapping data to reduce the number of pace-mapping data needed for future target VTs. This is made possible by a task-agnostic surrogate neural network that learns the mapping from pacing sites to 12-lead ECG morphology, an active-learning strategy that refines this surrogate model by selecting the most informative pacing site for each target, and a continual learning strategy to do so sequentially while retaining knowledge from prior targets. Evaluated on an in-silico testbed consisting of sequentially-presented localization tasks across different physiological conditions and ventricular geometries, cAPM with and without replay of past data samples achieved an 81% probability of localizing within clinical tolerance (5 mm accuracy) using 4.5 pace-mapping sites, compared to the state-of-the-art active-learning method achieving 38% probability using 13.7 pacing sites. These results provide a strong basis for preparing cAPM towards in-vivo preclinical and clinical studies where it can be used to guide pace-mapping.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一种物理约束框架，能够在无需预设数学形式的情况下，仅通过全场位移和力数据发现各向异性屈服函数，并确保其在弹塑性应力积分框架内的力学相容性，为材料本构模型的自动发现提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Identifying anisotropic yield functions remains challenging since yielding is not directly observed in full-field mechanical measurements, directional calibration can require many loading directions, and selecting an appropriate analytical form is nontrivial. The framework identifies the yield function as a mechanically constrained constitutive component inside elastoplastic stress integration, rather than through direct stress-space supervision. The yield function is represented by a convex neural network that enforces convexity and positive homogeneity of degree one while imposing the assumed tension-compression symmetry, and this neural yield function is trained with a differentiable stress update and a physics-informed force equilibrium loss across multiple loading cases. The proposed framework is validated using finite element (FE) benchmark studies with von Mises, Hill 1948, and Yld2000-2d yield functions, assessing yield contour agreement, displacement-noise sensitivity, identifiability through plastically active stress states, epistemic uncertainty, and polynomial-surrogate deployment. This study provides a mechanics-constrained pathway for discovering anisotropic yield functions from displacement and force data while keeping the identified component within the structure of elastoplastic stress integration.

Abstract: Scientific machine learning (SciML) has emerged as a promising approach for accelerating simulations of complex physical systems, yet achieving physically consistent and generalizable predictions for nonlinear, history-dependent problems remains a central challenge. In this study, we propose a hybrid GNN--FEM framework for efficient and generalizable phase-field fracture modeling. While phase-field approaches provide a robust variational framework for simulating complex crack evolution, their high computational cost limits practical applications because they require solving coupled, nonlinear, and history-dependent systems within an incremental finite element procedure. To address this challenge, a graph neural network surrogate is integrated into the conventional staggered scheme, replacing the phase-field update at each load increment while retaining the FEM-based displacement solver to enforce mechanical equilibrium and boundary conditions. By preserving the incremental solution structure, the framework remains consistent with history-dependent fracture evolution without requiring the surrogate to approximate the full solution trajectory. Numerical experiments demonstrate that the hybrid approach reduces computational cost while maintaining accuracy compared with conventional FEM, and exhibits robust predictive performance across diverse problem settings.

### [72] [How Linear Is a Transformer Feed-Forward Block? Per-Block Linear Recoverability Is Learned, Not Architectural](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19379)
*Stuart Whipp*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过最小二乘法量化了Transformer FFN的线性可恢复性，发现FFN的线性度是训练出来的特性而非架构使然，并利用该度量实现了有效的模型压缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer中的前馈网络（FFN）常被视为非线性计算模块，但其内部非线性的实际程度尚缺乏明确的量化度量。研究旨在揭示FFN块的线性化特征及其与模型性能、深度及架构的关系。

Method: 作者将Transformer FFN视为逐位置的输入到输出映射，通过闭式最小二乘法将其分解为线性部分和残差部分。通过计算线性映射解释的方差（R^2_lin）来量化其线性度，并利用该指标指导模型压缩。

Result: 研究发现：1. FFN的线性度在不同块之间高度异构且非单调，非线性并非由激活函数决定；2. 线性残差包含高阶或分布式结构，简单的双线性探针难以完全恢复；3. R^2_lin可作为有效的模型压缩指标，线性度高的块可用更小的线性层替代。

Conclusion: FFN的线性可恢复性（R^2_lin）是一种学到的、而非架构决定的属性。该研究强调了线性近似在分析Transformer FFN中的作用，并证明了基于线性可恢复性的模型压缩具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: Transformer feed-forward networks (FFNs) are often treated as nonlinear stores of computation, yet how nonlinear a trained FFN block actually is has rarely been measured. We treat each FFN as a position-wise input-to-output map and split it into the exact least-squares linear approximation plus a residual. The held-out variance the closed-form linear map explains defines a block's linear recoverability (R^2_lin), an optimiser-free measure of its linearity.
  Across all twelve blocks of GPT-2, Pythia-160m, and llama-160m, R^2_lin is highly heterogeneous and non-monotone with depth, ranging from near-linear (>0.99) to strongly nonlinear (<0.3) between adjacent blocks, and is not set by the activation function: same-width GELU models GPT-2 and Pythia-160m have sharply different profiles, so recoverability is a learned property of individual trained blocks, not an architectural one. A low-rank bilinear probe of the residual recovers only a few points of R^2, with gain uncorrelated with residual nonlinearity: the unrecovered computation is not a single position-wise product but higher-order or distributed structure.
  The measurement also serves as a targeted compression signal: recoverable blocks admit large single-layer replacements (GPT-2's early FFN at 8x fewer parameters for +0.77 perplexity), while low-recoverability blocks flag where this is unsafe. It further exposes a methodological pitfall: trained linear baselines can badly under-converge on ill-conditioned transformer activations, so we report the exact closed-form least-squares ceiling throughout.

</details>


### [73] [VERITAS: Verifier-Guided Proof Search for Zero-Shot Formal Theorem Proving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19399)
*Manish Acharya,Zhenyu Liao,Yueke Zhang,Kevin Leach,Yu Huang,Yifan Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VERITAS是一个通过两阶段协议将细粒度验证器反馈融入证明搜索的框架，有效提升了大模型在复杂数学定理证明中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大模型的形式化证明器往往将验证器反馈（如语法错误、类型不匹配等）简化为简单的“通过/失败”二元信号，导致丰富的纠错信息被浪费，限制了证明搜索的深度和成功率。

Method: 提出了一种名为VERITAS的两阶段证明搜索协议：第一阶段进行Best-of-N采样；第二阶段利用第一阶段失败的反馈信号作为负样本，通过评论家引导的蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）进行深度搜索。

Result: 在miniF2F基准测试中达到了40.6%的成功率（优于Best-of-5的36.9%和Portfolio的26.2%）；在自建的组合数学基准测试VERITAS-CombiBench中达到了7.3%（优于Portfolio的3.6%和Best-of-5的1.8%）。

Conclusion: VERITAS证明了利用形式化验证器中细粒度的反馈信号（而非仅仅是二元通过/失败信息）能够显著提升大模型在数学证明任务中的表现。该研究揭示了在复杂推理任务中，基于反馈的探索比简单的无指导采样更为有效。

Abstract: LLM-based formal provers often collapse rich verifier signals (syntax errors, type mismatches, partial goal progress) into a binary pass/fail bit. We present VERITAS, a zero-shot framework that routes every verifier signal back into proof search through a two-phase protocol: Best-of-N sampling first, then a critic-guided MCTS pass that ingests Phase 1 failures as explicit negative examples. The protocol preserves every theorem solved by its own Phase 1 sweep, so Phase 2's additional solves are attributable to feedback-driven exploration. VERITAS reaches 40.6% on miniF2F (vs. an independently run Best-of-5 at 36.9%, Portfolio 26.2%) and 7.3% on VERITAS-CombiBench, a 55-theorem combinatorics benchmark we release on which Best-of-5 (1.8%) falls below Portfolio (3.6%), exposing that unguided sampling hurts when correct lemma names must be recovered iteratively from verifier feedback. Artifacts are available on GitHub.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于注意力谱的幻觉检测方法通常仅依赖于少数特征值或手工选取的标量，导致大量关于模型推理质量的结构化信息被浪费。作者旨在利用统计力学框架，全面捕捉注意力拉普拉斯矩阵中蕴含的深度推理信息，以提升幻觉检测的准确性。

Method: 该论文提出了一种名为“自由能签名（Fes）”的光谱描述符，通过将注意力拉普拉斯矩阵视为哈密顿量，计算其热力学势（配分函数、自由能、光谱熵、热容）及随机矩阵理论（RMT）中的谱形状因子。研究人员还开发了一个基于这些描述符的轻量级探测器，并分析了其在有监督（训练探测器）和无监督（基于RMT偏差评分）环境下的表现。

Result: 在六个开源大模型和六个基准测试中，Fes 方法表现优异，平均 AUROC 指标较现有基线方法（如 LapEig 和 GoR-4）分别提升了 6.5 和 2.4 个百分点；在完全无监督的场景下，RMT 偏差得分亦能达到 0.71 的 AUROC。理论层面，该方法证明了 Lipschitz 稳定性、表达能力以及基于 PAC 的有限样本误差界限。

Conclusion: 该研究通过将自由能签名（Fes）引入大模型幻觉检测，证明了从统计力学视角提取注意力层特征的有效性。研究表明，正确生成表现出更接近 Wigner-Dyson 的谱统计特征，而幻觉则趋向于泊松分布。这种方法不仅提供了理论上的稳定性与收敛性保障，也为无需模型微调的轻量级检测开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Hallucination detection in large language models (LLMs) is deployment-critical, and recent work shows that the spectrum of attention-derived graph Laplacians carries strong signal about reasoning quality. Prior spectral diagnostics, however, summarize the Laplacian spectrum by a handful of eigenvalues or hand-picked scalars, leaving most of its structure unused. We propose Free-Energy Signatures (Fes), a spectral descriptor that treats each layer's attention Laplacian as a Hamiltonian and extracts its thermodynamic potentials partition function, free energy, spectral entropy, heat capacity together with the random-matrix-theory (RMT) spectral form factor. We prove three results: (i)~Lipschitz stability of Fes under attention perturbation; (ii)~an expressiveness result showing that Fes enriches finite spectral summaries and approximates moment-derived spectral functionals under explicit regularity and grid-resolution assumptions; and (iii)~a finite-sample PAC bound on the AUROC of a training-free detector built from Fes. Empirically, across six open-weight LLMs and six benchmarks, a lightweight probe on Fes descriptors achieves the strongest aggregate AUROC among attention-spectral baselines, improving over LapEig by $+6.5$ AUROC points and over GoR-4 by $+2.4$ points on average, while requiring no update to the underlying LLM. In the fully unsupervised setting, an RMT-deviation score achieves mean AUROC $0.71$, providing a label-free but weaker detector. A complementary RMT analysis shows that correct generations exhibit more Wigner-Dyson like spectral statistics, whereas hallucinations exhibit more Poisson-like statistics. The anonymized code and config are provided in the supplementary material.

</details>


### [75] [FlexLAM: Resolving the Bottleneck Trade-off in Latent Action Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19408)
*Takanori Yoshimoto,Yang Hu,Naruya Kondo,Tatsuya Matsushima*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FlexLAM 引入了可变长度的潜动作表示，通过嵌套 Dropout 训练克服了固定容量瓶颈的局限性，在不增加额外架构开销的前提下，实现了推理时动态调整动作精度，并显著提升了动作表征的质量与对齐能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有潜动作模型（LAMs）普遍采用固定容量的瓶颈设计，存在“瓶颈权衡”问题：过窄的编码可能丢失关键动作信息，而过宽的编码则引入了不必要的冗余变化，导致在标注稀缺时对齐困难。研究旨在解决这一固定瓶颈带来的灵活性缺失与表征效率低下的问题。

Method: 提出了 FlexLAM 架构，通过嵌套 Dropout（nested dropout）训练生成变长潜动作编码，形成前缀有效（prefix-valid）的编码空间。这种方法允许模型在训练时学习到从粗到细的动作表示结构，并在推理阶段根据需求动态调整潜空间动作的长度（Token 预算），而无需重新训练模型。

Result: 实验表明，FlexLAM 在标准稀缺标签监督及单任务对齐压力测试下，在各 Token 预算指标上均匹配或优于传统固定容量模型。此外，该模型支持推理时动态调整 Token 预算，并在 Ego4D 视频转换重构任务中表现出性能提升，证实了其作为“即插即用”升级方案的有效性。

Conclusion: FlexLAM 证明了变长潜空间动作表示是现有潜动作模型（LAMs）的一种高效且通用的升级方案。通过嵌套 Dropout 训练，模型无需额外架构调整即可实现推理时的动态精度调节，且在固定的 Token 预算下学习到了更优的动作表征，为视频动作建模与下游决策任务提供了更灵活的接口。

Abstract: Latent actions provide a compact interface between action-free video and downstream decision-making, yet existing Latent Action Models (LAMs) force every transition through a fixed-capacity bottleneck. We identify a bottleneck trade-off: overly tight codes can discard transition cues needed for action alignment, while overly loose codes preserve additional transition variation that must be resolved when alignment labels are scarce or narrowly distributed. FlexLAM replaces this fixed capacity with variable-length latent actions trained by nested dropout, yielding prefix-valid codes that capture compact transition structure first and add detail only when needed, without new architectures or losses. A single FlexLAM matches or surpasses separately trained fixed-capacity LAMs at every evaluated token budget under standard scarce-label supervision and under a low-return single-task alignment stress test, indicating that FlexLAM is not merely adjustable at inference time but learns a better latent-action interface at the same token budgets. The same model supports inference-time token-budget adjustment without retraining, and FlexLAM improves Ego4D transition reconstruction. These results suggest that variable-length latent actions are an architecture-free, drop-in upgrade to the fixed-capacity bottleneck in latent action models, latent-action world models, and video-pretrained action interfaces.

### [76] [Spectral DPPs via NEPv: A Scalable Continuous Relaxation of Determinantal MAP for Diversity-Aware Data Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19411)
*Richard Yi Da Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于流形优化和非线性特征值问题的DPP-MAP高效求解方法，通过自洽场迭代算法实现了在近线性时间内进行大规模数据多样性子集选择，克服了传统方法在高维海量数据下的计算限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模机器学习中，从海量候选集中选择高质量、多样性的子集（如数据策展、主动学习、提示选择等）至关重要。传统的DPP-MAP算法因其NP-hard特性及超线性的计算开销，难以应用于百万至十亿量级的数据规模，因此需要一种可扩展的、高效的多样性选择算法。

Method: 1. 将离散的DPP-MAP问题重构为Stiefel流形上的连续优化问题；2. 推导并分析该优化问题的非线性特征值问题（NEPv）形式；3. 设计了一种基于谱间隙局部收缩保证的自洽场（SCF）迭代求解器；4. 利用核函数的矩阵-向量乘法，将计算复杂度降低至近线性级别。

Result: 提出了一种名为“OurMethod”的高效求解算法，其计算复杂度为O((ndk+nk^2)t)，实现了对地面集合规模n的近线性扩展。该算法无需计算全核矩阵，通过矩阵-向量积即可完成迭代，有效解决了传统DPP在高维大数据场景下的计算瓶颈。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种将行列式点过程（DPP）MAP推理转化为Stiefel流形上的连续优化问题的新框架，并证明了该框架下的自洽场迭代算法具有良好的收敛性。该方法实现了在近线性时间内解决大规模数据子集选择问题，为处理海量候选集提供了有效的数学和算法基础。

Abstract: Selecting a small, diverse, high-quality subset from a massive pool of candidates is a recurring primitive in modern machine learning -- data curation and coreset selection for training and fine-tuning large models, active-learning batch acquisition, prompt and exemplar selection for in-context learning, retrieval diversification, and experimental design. Determinantal Point Processes (\DPP s) give a principled, well-calibrated notion of diversity for this task, but their \emph{MAP} objective -- pick a size-$k$ subset $S$ maximizing $\logdet(L_S)$ -- is NP-hard, and the standard greedy and sampling algorithms scale superlinearly in the ground-set size $n$. This cost is prohibitive precisely in the data-centric regime where diversity matters most, where $n$ ranges over millions to billions of candidate examples, features, or embeddings. We recast \DPP-MAP as a continuous optimization problem over the Stiefel manifold, and show that its first-order optimality conditions form a \emph{Nonlinear Eigenvalue Problem with eigenvector dependency} (\NEPv) of a previously unstudied form. This \NEPv\ admits a self-consistent field (\SCF) iteration with a spectral-gap-based local contraction guarantee, giving a principled iterative solver where the diversity objective drives an eigenvector-dependent operator. The resulting algorithm, \OurMethod, requires only matrix-vector products with the kernel and runs in time $O\!\big((ndk+nk^2)\,t\big)$ for a small number of iterations $t$, scaling near-linearly in $n$ and integrating directly with low-rank and feature-map kernels common in ML. This paper focuses on the relaxation, solver, and scaling analysis; full real-data benchmarking is left to a planned empirical study.

*Huu Hiep Nguyen,Minh Hoang Nguyen,Dung Nguyen,Hung Le*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有检索增强型时间序列预测方法存在“光谱盲点”（忽略频域特征）和“时间近因忽视”（对所有历史数据一视同仁）两大局限，难以有效处理非平稳时间序列的复杂模式。

Method: 1. 将时间序列转换为窗口化频域表示；2. 使用融合了幅值和相位信息的综合指标来衡量相似性；3. 引入指数移动平均（EMA）加权方案，以强调近期窗口数据的权重，从而平衡历史背景与近期趋势。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上的广泛实验表明，SpecReTF 在处理各种非平稳时间序列时，其预测精度显著优于传统的时间域检索方法。

Conclusion: SpecReTF 通过结合频域特征感知与时间衰减权重机制，有效解决了传统检索增强型时间序列预测方法在捕捉周期性结构和重视近期数据方面的不足，为处理复杂、非平稳时间序列提供了一种更优的解决方案。

Abstract: Time series forecasting leverages historical patterns to predict future values, but traditional methods face challenges when dealing with complex, non-stationary patterns that are difficult to memorize during training. Retrieval-augmented approaches have emerged as promising solutions by retrieving similar historical patterns to enhance predictions. However, existing retrieval methods suffer from two fundamental limitations: spectral blindness, which overlooks critical frequency-domain characteristics that capture underlying periodic structures, and temporal recency, which treats all historical data equally without emphasizing recent, more relevant patterns. In this paper, we propose SpecReTF, a novel retrieval method that addresses these issues by converting time series into windowed frequency representations, measuring similarity with a combined metric that captures both amplitude and phase information. To balance recency and historical context, we apply an exponential moving average weighting scheme that emphasizes recent windows. Extensive experiments on benchmark datasets demonstrate that SpecReTF outperforms time-domain retrieval methods, achieving superior forecasting accuracy across diverse, non-stationary time series.

### [78] [Does Text Actually Help? Uncovering and Resolving Text Collapse in Multimodal Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19413)
*Huu Hiep Nguyen,Minh Hoang Nguyen,Dung Nguyen,Hung Le*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多模态时间序列预测中常见的“文本崩塌”现象，本文提出 REST-TS 框架，通过强制文本分支仅对数值模型的预测残差进行建模，有效克服了数值输入主导带来的信息缺失问题，显著提升了预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态时间序列预测框架存在“文本崩塌（text collapse）”问题，即文本分支往往被数值分支的强自相关性所掩盖，导致文本分支未能提供有效的判别信息，模型无法充分利用多模态数据中的互补性知识。

Method: 提出一种名为 REST-TS（基于残差的文本监督）的新框架。该方法将数值分支与文本分支解耦，让数值分支独立进行预测，而文本分支被明确强制仅对数值分支无法解释的“残差”部分进行预测。这种设计强制文本分支必须从输入描述中提取实际内容，以最小化残差损失。

Result: 在多个真实世界领域和不同基准架构上的实验表明，REST-TS 达到了最先进（SOTA）的性能水平，并显著提高了文本分支的有效利用率，证实了残差监督策略在强制文本分支提取内容方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过针对预测残差进行监督学习，可以有效缓解多模态时间序列预测中文本分支的失效问题，强制模型挖掘文本中的增量知识，从而显著提升预测性能。

Abstract: Multimodal time series forecasting, which pairs numerical sequences with domain-relevant textual reports, promises to inject world knowledge into forecasting pipelines. However, we uncover a critical failure mode in existing frameworks that we term text collapse: the text branch converges to a content-independent transformation, contributing negligible discriminative signal regardless of the input description. We argue that text collapse is a consequence of a fundamental asymmetry in time series forecasting: the numerical input is strongly autocorrelated with the output, making the numerical backbone inherently dominant, while the text branch, despite carrying complementary and often critical information, is insufficiently utilized, leading to its systematic underexploitation. To address this, we propose \textbf{REST-TS} (\textbf{R}esidual-\textbf{E}xclusive \textbf{S}upervision for \textbf{T}ext in \textbf{T}ime \textbf{S}eries), which turns the asymmetry into a design principle: the numerical backbone produces its own independent numerical forecast, and the text branch is exclusively supervised to predict the structured components of the residual, the prediction gap that numbers cannot explain. Because no numerical pathway can reduce these losses, the text branch must extract genuine content from the input description. Evaluated across diverse real-world domains and backbone architectures, REST-TS achieves state-of-the-art performance and consistently demonstrates greater text-branch utilization than existing frameworks, providing strong empirical evidence that supervising the text branch on the residual compels it to extract genuine content from the input.

Abstract: Loan origination is the process by which a lender creates a new loan, from application and underwriting through approval and funding. Recently, firms have begun using mortgage loan agents to augment human loan officers, despite a lack of any public benchmark. To fill this gap, we present MortarBench, a loan origination agent benchmark. We find that state-of-the-art large language models (LLMs) perform poorly, with closed-source models achieving at most 77.1\% exact match accuracy. Abstract: We introduce 3D-DLP, a self-supervised object-centric representation learning model that decomposes scene-level RGB-D or voxel observations into a set of 3D latent particles. Building on the Deep Latent Particles (DLP) framework, each particle encodes disentangled attributes, including 3D keypoint position, bounding box dimensions, and appearance features, and represents a distinct entity in the scene. The model learns interpretable per-particle segmentation maps through an end-to-end self-supervised reconstruction objective. We demonstrate on both simulated and real-world datasets that the learned latent space is interpretable and controllable: by manipulating particle positions and decoding, we can generate novel scene configurations. Furthermore, we show that leveraging these compact 3D latent particles for downstream robotic manipulation improves performance over baselines that either lack explicit 3D information or rely on memory-intensive dense 3D inputs without object-centric structure. ### [81] [Can In-Context Learning Support Intrinsic Curiosity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19476)
*Eric Elmoznino,Sangnie Bhardwaj,Johannes von Oswald,Rajai Nasser,Blaise Agüera y Arcas,João Sacramento,Rif A. Saurous,Guillaume Lajoie*
