Method: 研究提出利用大模型内生的上下文学习（ICL）能力作为无需梯度更新的“世界模型”。该方法通过在上下文中进行预测误差分析和反事实操控来计算内在奖励，从而指导探索策略；并通过理论分析，分别探讨了该方法在通用MDP环境与非时间序列环境下的偏差性质与收敛性。

Result: 理论上证明了在通用MDP中，基于ICL的奖励无法无偏地估计学习进度；但在非时间序列任务（如主动学习、贝叶斯实验设计）中，ICL推导出的奖励可以有效界定并渐近收敛于真实学习进度。实验结果表明，该框架能在多种环境下成功训练出具有“好奇心”且探索最优的数据采集策略。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论证明与实验验证，确立了上下文学习（ICL）在特定环境下评估“学习进度”的可行性。虽然在通用马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中存在偏见限制，但在主动学习和贝叶斯实验设计等非时间序列任务中，基于ICL的奖励机制能够有效收敛至真实学习进度，为高效的自动化数据选择提供了理论支持。

Abstract: Effective machine learning depends not only on how we model data, but also on what data we choose to collect. While large sequence models have revolutionized data modeling, the problem of automated data selection, or "intrinsic curiosity", remains a significant challenge. Classic approaches incentivize exploration by rewarding an agent based on its "learning progress", which measures how much a newly acquired observation improves a world model's predictive ability. However, evaluating these rewards traditionally requires expensive inner loops of gradient descent updates within each trajectory, rendering them computationally impractical at scale. In this work, we investigate whether the emergent in-context learning (ICL) capabilities of sequence models can eliminate this bottleneck by serving as immediate, update-free world models. Specifically, we evaluate whether an exploration policy can be trained to maximize learning progress, using solely the prediction errors and counterfactual context manipulations of an in-context learner. We first prove that in general Markov decision processes, this is in fact impossible in an unbiased way: the resulting intrinsic rewards either suffer from nuisance terms that bias their estimation of true learning progress, or they cannot be implemented using an in-context learner's prediction errors. Conversely, we prove a positive result for a broad subclass of non-temporal settings, encompassing active learning and Bayesian Experimental Design: here, ICL-derived rewards successfully bound and asymptotically converge to the true learning progress. We corroborate our theory with controlled experiments across continuous and symbolic environments, demonstrating that our ICL-driven framework successfully trains curious data-collection policies that explore optimally.

</details>

Discretisation creates fictional representations of complex clinical scenarios and compromises the generalisability of retrospective model evaluations. ### [83] [Concept Flow Models: Anchoring Concept-Based Reasoning with Hierarchical Bottlenecks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19489)
*Ya Wang,Adrian Paschke*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对传统概念瓶颈模型存在的信息泄露问题，本文提出了概念流模型（CFM），通过层次化的决策树结构将概念处理细化，在保障预测性能的同时提升了模型的可解释性与安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的概念瓶颈模型（CBM）在减少人工标注方面取得了进展，但当概念数量增多时会引发严重的信息泄露问题，导致模型利用虚假或无关的相关性进行预测，从而削弱了可解释性。

Method: 提出概念流模型（CFM），利用分层、概念驱动的决策树替代传统的平面瓶颈结构。其核心方法包括：1. 从视觉嵌入中构建决策层次结构；2. 在每一层级分配语义概念；3. 通过概率树遍历训练可微的概念权重，从而实现逐步细化的决策过程。

Result: 在多个基准测试上的实验表明，CFM不仅能达到与平面CBM相当的预测准确率，而且显著降低了有效概念的使用率，有效缓解了信息泄露，并提供了清晰、分层的决策路径。

Conclusion: 概念流模型（CFM）通过层次化决策结构有效解决了传统瓶颈模型中由于概念维度过高导致的信息泄露问题，在保持预测性能的同时，极大地增强了模型决策过程的透明度与可审计性。

Abstract: Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) enhance interpretability by projecting learned features into a human-understandable concept space. Recent approaches leverage vision-language models to generate concept embeddings, reducing the need for manual concept annotations. However, these models suffer from a critical limitation: as the number of concepts approaches the embedding dimension, information leakage increases, enabling the model to exploit spurious or semantically irrelevant correlations and undermining interpretability. In this work, we propose Concept Flow Models (CFMs), which replace the flat bottleneck with a hierarchical, concept-driven decision tree. Each internal node in the hierarchy focuses on a localized subset of discriminative concepts, progressively narrowing the prediction scope. Our framework constructs decision hierarchies from visual embeddings, distributes semantic concepts at each hierarchy level, and trains differentiable concept weights through probabilistic tree traversal. Extensive experiments on diverse benchmarks demonstrate that CFMs match the predictive performance of flat CBMs, while substantially mitigating information leakage by reducing effective concept usage. Furthermore, CFMs yield stepwise decision flows that enable transparent and auditable model reasoning with hierarchical class structures.

### [84] [Algebraic Dead Directions in LayerNorm Transformers: A Forward-Pass-Only Diagnostic at LLM Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19491)
*Tejas Pradeep Shirodkar,P. J. Narayanan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需前向传播即可从LayerNorm参数直接识别Transformer“死方向”的代数方法，揭示了Transformer损失函数中存在的固有奇异几何结构，并验证了其在归一化机制识别和模型分析中的应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练Transformer通常处于损失函数的奇异极小值附近，其Fisher信息矩阵在特定“死方向”上发生退化。现有的识别这些方向的方法（如前向传播结合特征分解或采样估计）计算成本高昂，无法仅从模型参数本身获得。因此，作者旨在寻找一种仅依赖模型参数即可高效解析LayerNorm Transformer特定奇异结构的方法。

Method: 利用LayerNorm仿射参数的逆尺度向量（inverse-scale direction）作为后终层归一化（post-final-norm）中心化激活协方差矩阵的精确代数核。通过该方法，无需任何数据输入、前向/反向传播或特征值分解，即可直接计算出模型参数空间中的死方向。研究者在14个不同规模和目标的预训练Transformer上验证了该理论的准确性。

Result: 在9个LayerNorm模型中，所预测的方向与通过单次前向传播测得的奇异方向在随机初始化时精度高达四位小数；在5个RMSNorm模型中，由于缺乏平均减法投影算子，该方向被正确排除。实验还发现，随着训练深入，该方向的协方差特征值会显著下降（约10^3倍），且出现更多死方向。此外，该方法可用于解释残差流奇异值的保持规律及从参数中识别归一化类型。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种无需前向或反向传播即可直接从LayerNorm参数中识别预训练Transformer“死方向”（dead directions）的代数方法。研究揭示了LayerNorm架构固有的奇异性，并证明了该特性在模型评估、正则化识别及残差流奇异值分析中的有效性，为理解模型参数空间的几何结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: Pretrained transformers sit near singular minima of the loss, where the Fisher information metric degenerates along dead directions: directions in parameter space along which the directional Fisher vanishes. Locating such a direction normally needs a forward pass and an eigendecomposition of activations, or a sampling-based complexity estimate; none returns a direction computable from the network's parameters alone. We give one, for LayerNorm transformers. The inverse-scale direction $γ^{-1}/\|γ^{-1}\|$ of the LayerNorm affine is an exact algebraic kernel of the post-final-norm centred activation covariance, for any input distribution, and induces a corresponding dead direction in parameter space. It is read from the LN scale parameter alone, with no forward or backward pass and no eigensolve: the cheapest dead-direction read, specific to LayerNorm. We test it on $14$ pretrained transformers ($9$ LayerNorm, $5$ RMSNorm; $160$M-$35$B; language and vision objectives). At random initialisation the predicted direction matches the measured bottom singular direction (one forward pass, direct SVD) to four decimal places on $9/9$ LayerNorm models, and is correctly absent on $5/5$ RMSNorm models, which lack the mean-subtraction projector that creates it. On the trained checkpoint the covariance eigenvalue along this direction deepens by ${\sim}10^3\times$ and further dead directions open; the random-init-to-trained gap is a one-forward-pass, per-checkpoint readout of singular structure along the predicted coordinate. Two consequences follow in closed form: the residual stream's smallest singular value is preserved block-to-block on $13/14$ transformers measured on their own input distribution, the one exception (Gemma$4$-$31$B) a genuine dead direction the same read pinpoints; and the kernel direction's presence classifies a transformer's normalisation from the parameters alone.

</details>


### [85] [Calibrating Generative Models to Feature Distributions with MMD Finetuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19496)
*Nathaniel L. Diamant,Brian L. Trippe*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: kCGM 是一种新型生成模型校准框架，通过最小化 MMD 和 KL 正则化，在不牺牲样本有效性的前提下，有效纠正了生成模型在关键特征分布上的偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生成模型虽然能产生看似合理的样本，但往往在关键特征分布上与目标集合存在显著偏差。传统的直接微调方法容易导致模型过拟合，且无法精确控制匹配的特征维度，导致生成的分子或序列在有效性与分布对齐之间难以平衡。因此需要一种更精细的校准方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 kernel Calibrating Generative Models (kCGM) 的方法。该方法通过使用无偏得分函数估计器（unbiased score-function estimator）最小化生成样本特征分布与目标数据集特征分布之间的最大均值差异（MMD），同时引入 KL 散度正则化以确保模型参数不偏离预训练模型太远，从而实现分布校准。

Result: 在 174 种抗生素数据集的实验中，kCGM 相比直接微调在提升目标特征匹配度的同时，提高了分子的化学有效性。此外，该方法在蛋白质和 DNA 生成任务中展现了良好的适应性，成功校准了自回归模型、连续空间扩散模型和离散扩散模型。

Conclusion: kCGM 提供了一种有效的分布校准框架，能够在仅利用特征级监督的情况下，通过最小化 MMD 并辅以 KL 正则化，引导生成模型在保持样本多样性和有效性的同时，精准对齐目标分布。该方法具备良好的通用性，适用于多种生成模型架构及生物分子生成任务。

Abstract: Generative models can produce individually plausible samples while deviating substantially from a target set in the distribution of key features. For example, a model pretrained on broad drug-like chemical space may generate molecules whose molecular features differ from those of a therapeutic class of interest, such as known antibiotics. Correcting such distributional miscalibration is challenging: direct finetuning on the target set can overfit and does not control which features are matched. To fill this gap, we introduce kernel Calibrating Generative Models (kCGM). kCGM minimizes a maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) between generated and target feature distributions using an unbiased score-function estimator, with KL regularization to remain close to the pretrained model. On a target set of 174 antibiotics, direct finetuning sacrifices chemical validity for feature-distribution matching, whereas kCGM improves target feature matching while increasing validity. We further demonstrate kCGM in protein and DNA generation tasks, showing it can adapt autoregressive, continuous-space diffusion, and discrete diffusion models using only feature-level supervision. Code is available at https://github.com/smithhenryd/cgm.

### [86] [Interactive Pareto navigation for deep multi-task learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19521)
*Augustina C. Amakor,Konstantin Sonntag,Sebastian Peitz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为PPE的新框架，旨在多任务学习中通过预测-校正方法交互式地探索帕累托最优解，利用Krylov子空间方法高效处理决策偏好，有效解决了传统方法计算成本高且难以捕捉复杂帕累托前沿的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多任务学习中目标增多会导致计算资源需求剧增且难以平衡，传统的加权和损失函数方法难以处理复杂的帕累托前沿形状，且在深度学习场景下多次调整计算的代价过高。

Method: 提出了“偏好帕累托探索”（PPE）框架，采用预测-校正（predictor-corrector）方法，在帕累托最优流形上进行切线预测，并结合Krylov子空间方法（仅需矩阵-向量积，无需显式计算海森矩阵）来刻画切空间，从而在保持计算效率的同时有效地整合决策者的偏好。

Result: 实验证明，PPE框架在玩具问题和深度学习任务中均表现出良好的性能，能够在交互式探索过程中有效捕捉并满足决策者的偏好，同时避免了高昂的海森矩阵计算成本。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的PPE框架有效解决了多目标优化中决策偏好难以平衡以及帕累托前沿探索计算成本高昂的问题，为深度学习中的多任务优化提供了一种高效且可交互的解决方案。

Abstract: In multi-task learning, handling an increasing number of objectives can quickly become challenging, both in terms of the computational resources and the decision maker's capacity to choose appropriate trade-offs. A widely used approach is thus to aggregate the individual losses in a single loss function by a weighted sum. This often fails to capture either the decision maker's preferences as a result of the shape of the Pareto front, or requires multiple adjustments and computations which becomes prohibitively expensive in deep learning applications. To address these issues, we introduce a novel framework, Preference Pareto Exploration (PPE), which enforces the decision maker's preferences while accounting for the geometry of the Pareto set in an interactive exploration process. PPE is based on a predictor-corrector method that performs predictor steps tangential to the manifold of Pareto-optimal solutions, following the decision maker's preference. The subsequent corrector step results in a new trade-off reflecting this preference. To avoid explicit Hessian computations when characterizing the tangent space of the manifold, we employ a Krylov subspace method that relies solely on matrix-vector products. These products can be efficiently obtained via automatic differentiation, ensuring both efficiency and robustness throughout the optimization process. The method's functionality and performance are demonstrated using both toy problems and examples from deep learning.

Abstract: Fine-tuning of Large Language Models (LLMs) using Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) on an end-user's data offers personalized experiences while keeping data private, but faces severe memory constraints on consumer hardware. Peak memory during fine-tuning often exceeds device limits, especially for models with billions of parameters and long-context training data. This paper introduces a suite of complementary techniques to reduce memory footprint without sacrificing model quality: (1) base model quantization with on-the-fly dequantization, (2) memory-efficient checkpointing combining selective activation caching and disk offloading, (3) softmax approximation using semantically relevant token subsets, and (4) logits masking. ### [88] [Tracking Representation Dynamics in Large Language Models with Persistent Homology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19542)
*Naman Malhotra,Jay Ambadkar,Abhinav Gupta,Kushal Kasivel,Abbas Schwarz,Kamillo Ferry,Anthea Monod*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管监督微调是主流对齐方式，但其过程中模型内部表示的演化机制尚不明确，缺乏对模型内部状态在微调期间拓扑演化规律的深入研究。

Method: 利用持久同调（Persistent Homology）技术，通过追踪大语言模型在有监督微调（SFT）过程中激活空间的拓扑结构变化，对比了不同参数规模（1B至7B）及不同对齐目标（有用性、无害性及混合数据）下的演化动力学。

Result: 研究发现：1. 大部分拓扑重组发生在训练初期；2. 密集检查点分析显示，拓扑活跃度存在短暂峰值后迅速稳定；3. 不同的对齐目标会诱导产生可区分的拓扑轨迹；4. 指令微调模型与预训练模型表现出本质不同的拓扑演化模式。

Conclusion: 持久同调为理解大语言模型对齐过程提供了有效的分析视角，揭示了模型在表示层面的演化规律，这不仅能补充行为学指标的不足，也为未来优化模型训练动力学提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Large language models are commonly aligned through supervised fine-tuning, yet little is known about how their internal representations evolve during this process. We study alignment dynamics using persistent homology by tracking the topology of activation spaces throughout fine-tuning. Across four transformer language models ranging from 1B to 7B parameters and three alignment objectives corresponding to helpful, harmless, and mixed training data, we find that the majority of topological reorganization occurs during the earliest stages of training. A dense checkpoint analysis reveals a transient peak in topological activity followed by rapid stabilization. We further show that different alignment objectives induce distinguishable topological trajectories, while instruction-tuned and pretrained models exhibit qualitatively different patterns of evolution. Our results suggest that persistent homology provides a complementary perspective on alignment, revealing representation-level changes that are not apparent from behavioral metrics alone.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LoRA 适配器合并通常在训练结束后才进行评估，由于不同任务的适配器之间可能存在破坏性的相互干扰，导致后期发现合并效果不佳，造成昂贵的计算资源浪费。因此，研究者旨在探索是否能在训练早期预测适配器的“可合并性”。

Method: 提出了 MergeProbe 框架，通过在训练初期（前几个百分点）监测低秩更新与梯度在跨任务间的对齐情况，以及对共享表示的扰动程度，来预测适配器的合并性能，并据此采取直接合并、重加权、剪枝或路由等决策。

Result: 在 MERGE-PEFT 基准测试上，MergeProbe 在平均性能保持和最差情况下的保持力方面均优于现有的抗干扰合并基线，且部署开销远低于全任务路由方案。

Conclusion: MergeProbe 将 LoRA 合并从传统的后期工程阶段转变为一种可预测的测量问题，在保证高性能的同时显著降低了合并带来的干预风险和计算开销。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation (LoRA) makes it cheap to train many domain- and task-specific language model adapters, but whether two adapters can be merged is usually discovered only after both have been fully trained and evaluated. This late feedback is costly: adapters that are strong in isolation can interfere destructively once their updates are combined. We ask whether this outcome can be anticipated. We formalize adapter mergeability as the degree to which an adapter preserves its single-task utility after merging, and show that it can be forecast from signals measured in the first few percent of training -- chiefly how the low-rank updates and their gradients align across tasks and how much they disturb shared representations. We package these signals into MergeProbe, a lightweight predictor that estimates pairwise and set-level retention and turns the estimate into a concrete decision: merge directly, reweight, prune, or route. On MERGE-PEFT, a five-domain benchmark spanning math, code, science, instruction following, and safety, MergeProbe attains the best average and worst-case retention among strong interference-aware merge baselines while adding far less deployment overhead than full task routing. This turns LoRA merging from a post-hoc engineering step into an anticipatory measurement problem.

</details>


### [90] [Displacement Is Not Direction: Evaluating Fidelity Metrics for Quantized LLM Deployment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19558)
*Miloš Nikolić,Ali Hadi Zadeh,Enrique Torres Sanchez,Andreas Moshovos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 保真度指标（如KL散度）不能作为量化模型下游质量的可靠代理指标，尤其是在高精度模型序列中，其相关性会完全失效，且在预测具体任务失败方面表现欠佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 保真度指标（如每标记KL散度）常被视为一种低成本的基准测试替代方案，用以评估量化后模型与原始模型的一致性。本文旨在通过实证研究验证这种做法在实际应用中的有效性及其局限性。

Method: 研究者使用两个量化模型序列（Qwen3.6-35B-A3B和Devstral-Small-2-24B），通过分析KL散度与下游基准测试成绩的相关性，测试了14种保真度度量指标变体。同时，在LiveCodeBench数据集上进行了逐提示（per-prompt）层面的失败预测实验和跨模型路由准确性评估，并通过结构分解分析了KL散度与模型性能表现之间的关联本质。

Result: 研究发现，虽然KL散度在整个量化区间内与基准测试分数表现出强相关性，但在“静默区”（near-baseline silent zone）相关性彻底崩溃（无统计学意义）。在逐提示级别上，KL散度对代码生成失败的预测能力较弱，作为跨模型路由器的表现仅处于随机水平（42.3%-49.4%）。分析表明，KL散度主要衡量的是与参考模型的分歧总量，而非分歧的具体方向，因此无法准确反映模型性能的微小差异。

Conclusion: 尽管KL散度等保真度指标在评估整体量化模型时表现出较强的相关性，但在模型达到一定精度（即“静默区”）后会失效。此外，此类指标在预测特定任务失败或作为跨模型路由策略时效果不佳。这表明保真度指标无法完全替代下游基准测试，因为它们往往捕捉的是差异的体量而非差异的质量或方向。

Abstract: Fidelity metrics, such as per-token KL divergence (KLD) against a high-precision reference, are often used in practice as low-cost proxies for benchmark quality. We test this practice on a 28-quant cohort of Qwen3.6-35B-A3B and a 41-quant cohort of Devstral-Small-2-24B, evaluated across a suite of downstream benchmarks. We find that KLD is strongly correlated with benchmark score over the full cohort ($ρ=-0.72$ on Qwen and $ρ=-0.86$ on Devstral, both with $p<0.001$). However, this relationship collapses to non-significance in the near-baseline silent zone ($ρ=+0.00$ on Qwen and $ρ=-0.24$, $p=0.36$, on Devstral). This collapse persists across 14 measurement variants, including different KLD aggregations, perplexity formulations, top-1 agreement, calibration corpora, and context lengths. At the per-prompt level, KLD has only weak failure-prediction power on code, with failed-vs-passed geometric-mean ratios in $[1.08,1.22]$ across five models on LiveCodeBench, and fails as a cross-model router, achieving only $42.3\%-49.4\%$ accuracy on disagreement prompts. We trace the collapse to a structural decomposition: KLD primarily measures the volume of disagreement with the reference, with silent-zone composite $ρ=+0.94$ ($p<0.001$) on Qwen and $+0.55$ ($p=0.03$) on Devstral, while its relationship to the direction of those disagreements is weak and task-conditional.

</details>

Abstract: Seasonal influenza infects millions of people and causes substantial morbidity and mortality in the United States each year, making accurate short-term forecasting a core public-health need. Across tasks, we demonstrate that a mixture-of-experts model that fuses multiple pretrained forecasters achieves the strongest overall performance, indicating that heterogeneous pretrained representations provide complementary predictive information. Our results further show that numerical transformer-based models produce reliable forecasts, while pretraining provides the largest gains at longer horizons, particularly when the pretraining domain is mechanistically aligned with influenza dynamics. In contrast, LLM-based time series methods underperform relative to numerical forecasters in this setting. Finally, we examine hospitalization information as both an auxiliary covariate and a pretraining source. ### [92] [Advances in Scientific Machine Learning for Coupled Fluid Flow and Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19562)
*Gabriel F. Barros,Rômulo M. Silva,Alvaro L. G. A. Coutinho*

Main category: cs.LG

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 综述了多种SciML方法，包括基于奇异值分解的线性降阶技术（如动态模态分解，DMD），以及非线性神经网络方法（如物理信息神经网络PINNs和β-变分自编码器β-VAEs）。此外，研究结合了高性能计算策略（如自适应网格细化AMR/C和科学浮点数据压缩），并针对浊流和热对流场景提出了具体的替代建模方案。

Conclusion: 科学机器学习（SciML）为处理复杂流体流动与传输系统的建模提供了高效途径。尽管在实时预测和不确定性量化方面仍面临挑战，但在特定数据环境下，SciML能够在保持高精度的同时，显著降低全阶计算模拟的成本。

Abstract: This chapter reviews recent advances in Scientific Machine Learning (SciML) for modeling coupled fluid flow and transport phenomena governed by the incompressible Navier-Stokes and scalar transport equations. Such systems, found in applications like turbidity currents and thermal convection, feature strong nonlinear coupling and multiscale behavior that make high-fidelity simulations computationally expensive. To address this, the chapter surveys state-of-the-art SciML methods for building efficient surrogate models, including linear reduced-order techniques based on Singular Value Decomposition (such as Dynamic Mode Decomposition) and nonlinear neural network approaches like Physics-Informed Neural Networks (PINNs) and $β$-Variational Autoencoders ($β$-VAEs). It first covers the authors' work combining these models with High Performance Computing strategies, including Adaptive Mesh Refinement/Coarsening (AMR/C) and scientific floating-point data compression. It then presents two new contributions: surrogate modeling of turbidity currents via PINNs, and the extraction of disentangled nonlinear modes from thermal flows using $β$-VAEs. Governing equations and representative benchmarks, including lock-exchange flows and Rayleigh-Bénard convection, illustrate these methodologies. The chapter is intentionally long, covering both the mathematical and physical foundations of coupled fluid flow and the computational aspects of state-of-the-art modeling. Overall, it demonstrates how SciML enables fast, accurate approximations of complex coupled systems within the specific data regimes and modeling assumptions considered, while substantially reducing computational cost relative to full-order simulations. Broader capabilities such as real-time prediction and uncertainty quantification remain active research directions whose feasibility depends strongly on the problem at hand.

### [93] [On the QUEST for Uncertainty Quantification via Highest Density Regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19569)
*Sam Goring,Tom Kuipers,Nicola Paoletti,David S. Watson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的不确定性量化方法QUEST，通过分析分布的最高密度区域体积来刻画不确定性，克服了传统评分规则在非条件期望场景下的局限性，并展现出更好的理论公理性与实际预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的标量不确定性量化（UQ）方法主要基于适当评分规则（proper scoring rules）度量点预测风险。当目标统计量非条件期望时，这些方法往往会产生违背直觉的结果，且缺乏对认知不确定性和偶然不确定性的明确区分和理想的公理化性质。

Method: 提出了一种名为QUEST（Quantifying Uncertainty via highest dEnSiTy regions）的新方法。该方法不依赖于逐点预测风险（点估计），而是通过计算分布支持集内最可能子集的体积（即Lebesgue测度的集中度）来量化不确定性，并引入鲁棒性参数α进行评估。

Result: 研究表明，QUEST在理论上满足不确定性量化的关键公理（如分布离散时的单调性和对位置平移的不变性），并与信息论和经济学中的经典统计量建立了联系。在选择性预测基准测试中，QUEST在性能上优于方差和微分熵等标准度量。

Conclusion: QUEST提供了一种基于最高密度区域（Highest Density Regions）的强大不确定性量化框架，能够更直观且符合公理化要求地刻画不确定性，是回归任务中优于传统评分规则的替代方案。

Abstract: Uncertainty quantification (UQ) is essential for reliable decision-making in safety-critical applications in probabilistic machine learning. For regression problems, dominant scalar UQ approaches - notably, those based on proper scoring rules - measure uncertainty via pointwise predictive risk. This can lead to counterintuitive results when the target statistic is not the conditional expectation. We propose an alternative framework, in which uncertainty is characterised by the volume of the most probable subset of a distribution's support. QUEST (Quantifying Uncertainty via highest dEnSiTy regions) is a novel approach to UQ based on the concentration of Lebesgue measure at a distribution's peak(s), evaluated at one or more values of a robustness parameter $α$. We establish connections between our measures and classical statistics from information theory and economics. We show that, unlike popular alternatives based on proper scoring rules, QUEST measures of epistemic and aleatoric uncertainty satisfy a set of axioms adapted from the UQ literature, including monotonicity under distributional spread and invariance to location shifts. Selective prediction benchmarks confirm that QUEST performs favourably against standard measures such as variance and differential entropy.

  We introduce IHBench (Interruption Handling Benchmark), a benchmark that evaluates post-interruption recovery in voice agents executing state-machine-driven workflows across 10 enterprise domains. Across our experiments, closed-weight models are consistently more robust to interruptions than open-weight ones: they win far more often on task fulfillment, degrade roughly 3.3x more slowly as conversations grow longer, and show no audio-versus-text modality gap, whereas the open-weight models lose ground on all three. ### [96] [Comparing Linear Probes with Mahalanobis Cosine Similarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19603)
*Zhuofan Josh Ying,Peter Hase,Nikolaus Kriegeskorte*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出并验证了马氏余弦相似度（MCS）作为线性探测器性能评估指标的有效性，证明了MCS与OOD AUROC之间的线性关系，并为模型可解释性提供了强有力的理论支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的欧几里得余弦相似度在评估线性探测器时存在局限性，不能很好地反映探测器在分布外（OOD）环境下的表现。研究者旨在引入考虑测试数据协方差的马氏余弦相似度（MCS），以更好地解释探测器性能与OOD预测能力之间的关系。

Method: 该研究通过扩展经验实验（涵盖不同模型、层和概念领域）验证了MCS与OOD AUROC之间的线性关系，并构建了数学模型：假设类别分布为高斯分布，推导证明了两者之所以呈线性关系，是因为它们都是信噪比（SNR）的Sigmoid函数；同时，该理论还预测了这种线性关系失效的边界条件，并通过实验进行了验证。

Result: 研究证实了探测器的MCS与其在OOD数据上的性能（AUROC）之间存在近乎完美的线性预测关系（R² = 0.98），并从数学理论上证明了该现象的普适性，同时明确了该线性关系的适用范围与失效条件。

Conclusion: 马氏余弦相似度（MCS）是衡量线性探测器性能的理论基础更扎实且经验效果更好的指标。它不仅揭示了模型探测能力与OOD性能之间的内在联系，也为模型可解释性研究提供了一种新的量化评估工具。

Abstract: Linear probes are widely used in interpretability research and often compared by cosine similarity. The Mahalanobis cosine similarity (MCS) between two directions, which reweights the inner product by test data covariance, is a natural task-aware refinement. Ying et al. (2026) report that a probe's MCS to a reference probe trained on the out-of-distribution (OOD) data near-perfectly linearly predicts the probe's OOD AUROC (R^2 = 0.98). Here, we extend this empirical finding across models, layers, and concept domains, and prove this general phenomenon in closed form: For balanced classes whose projections are Gaussian, OOD AUROC and MCS to the reference probe are linear because both are sigmoid-shaped functions of the probe's signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) on the test data. The theory also predicts when this linearity fails, which we verify empirically. MCS offers a theoretically grounded and empirically effective alternative to Euclidean cosine similarity for comparing linear probes.

</details>


### [97] [Latent Confounded Causal Discovery via Lie Bracket Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19610)
*Sridhar Mahadevan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于范畴论与微分几何的因果发现新范式，通过分析观测与干预测度间的几何残差（BRIDGE算法）及谱流匹配（SKFM算法），在存在潜在混淆因子的情况下，有效降低了因果结构发现的搜索复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统因果发现算法在存在潜在混淆因子时，因搜索空间呈超指数级增长而面临极大挑战。本文旨在利用Kan-Do-Calculus（KDC）中观测与干预的范畴论二重伴随关系，通过微分几何手段（如Lie括号与流场分析）更有效地识别因果结构。

Method: 1. BRIDGE算法：利用Radon-Nikodym导数与Lie括号计算Frobenius残差，通过几何筛选排除不相容结构，缩小因果图搜索空间。2. SKFM算法：结合流匹配技术，通过学习干预场并进行谱分解，以端到端方式提取潜在结构。

Result: 实验结果表明，BRIDGE和SKFM算法能够显著缩小因果图（DAG）的搜索空间（多个数量级），并能准确识别包含潜在混淆因子的复杂因果模型，验证了基于干预诱导流进行结构发现的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文通过将因果发现重新构建为几何与范畴论问题，成功证明了干预诱导流的几何属性可以有效识别潜在混淆因子，为解决高维因果结构搜索问题提供了强有力的数学框架。

Abstract: Recent work on Kan-Do-Calculus (KDC) has established that the boundary between passive observation and active intervention in causal inference is a category-theoretic bi-adjunction, with interventions modeled by left Kan extensions and conditioning by right Kan extensions. This paper introduces two causal discovery algorithms under latent confounding, building on the information-geometric and categorical consequences of KDC. In smooth statistical settings, Radon-Nikodym derivatives between observational and interventional measures induce local causal vector fields; failures of these fields to close under Lie brackets become computable Frobenius residuals, which we interpret as witnesses of failed visible integrability and possible latent or unmodeled structure. Our first algorithm, BRIDGE (Bracket Residuals for Interventional Discovery and Geometric Estimation), combines an interventional density or Radon-Nikodym-ratio engine with a geometric screen that proposes a high-recall family of admissible arrows, identifies non-closing visible pairs as latent-obstruction candidates, and passes the reduced family to downstream score-based or differentiable discovery routines. The second algorithmic contribution, Spectral Kan-Do Flow Matching (SKFM), learns amortized intervention fields and factors latent curvature spectrally, exposing the direct Lie-space endpoint toward which BRIDGE points. A detailed set of experiments show that both algorithms are capable of discovering causal models with latent confounders while collapsing the super-exponential space of possible DAGs by many orders of magnitude. This paper introduces a new paradigm in causal discovery, where latent structure is inferred directly from the geometry of intervention-induced flows.

### [98] [SEAGAN: domain-Specific and Edge-Aware Graph Attention Network for Dynamic Plant Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19623)
*Antriksh Srivastava,Soumyashree Kar*

Main category: cs.LG

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为SEAGAN（面向动态植物过程的领域专用边感知图注意力网络）的框架。该方法将A-Ci曲线上的点视为图节点，利用基于距离的k最近邻（kNN）和辅助信号引导（ASG）构建图结构，并通过引入边属性、图注意力机制以及加权交叉熵损失函数来处理复杂的生化限制状态分类任务。

Abstract: Graph neural networks (GNNs) provide a flexible framework for learning from scientific data linked through physical, biological, or functional relationships. One promising domain is plant physiology, where measured responses often arise from multiple interacting processes whose exact separation remains difficult even with manual intervention. In plant physiology, a key example is the A-Ci curve, which relates net CO2 assimilation rate (Anet) to leaf intercellular CO2 concentration (Ci) and is used to estimate photosynthetic parameters in leaf and crop-canopy models. Here, we formulate limitation-state identification along A-Ci curves as a graph-based node classification problem, with curve points as nodes. The framework was evaluated against conventional learning baselines, graph-based architectures, and an automated fitting-based benchmark. Results on a large synthetic dataset with known ground-truth limitation states show that graph-based models improve classification, particularly near biochemical transition regions. The best-performing configuration, SEAGAN (domain-Specific and Edge-Aware Graph Attention Network for Dynamic Plant Processes), integrates process-aware node features, edge attributes, kNN connectivity, and graph attention with weighted cross-entropy loss, achieving an F1-score of 0.857 and an accuracy of 0.882. *Hongxuan Liu,Roman Bushuiev,Ivy Lightheart,Mrunali Manjrekar,Anton Bushuiev,Magdalena Lederbauer,Filip Jozefov,Yinkai Wang,Soha Hassoun,Josef Sivic,James Taylor,Runzhong Wang,David Healey,Tomáš Pluskal,Connor W. Coley*

Abstract: Reliable benchmarking is critical for developing machine learning models for tandem mass spectrometry (MS/MS) based molecule discovery. We distill our findings into recommendations generalizable to MS/MS challenges, benchmarks, and custom evaluation setups. ### [100] [Hard or Just Unreached? Diagnosing the Sampling Blind Spot in Math-Reasoning Difficulty Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19636)
*Luca Zhou,Sajel Shah,Emanuele Rodolà,Roberto Dessì*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文发现主流的数学评估指标 pass@k 存在严重盲点：许多模型在常规采样下无法解决的极难数学题，实际上可以通过微小的内部状态扰动（激活移植）被有效破解，证明了模型内部蕴含的推理能力被现有评估范式严重低估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数学与科学推理基准目前主要依赖 pass@k 指标来评估任务难度。然而，研究者注意到该指标在处理最困难的样本（即在有限尝试下完全无法解决的问题）时存在显著的盲点。作者旨在揭示并量化这一缺陷，探讨模型在传统评估框架下表现出的“能力受限”是否源于推理路径的僵化，而非模型本身知识的缺失。

Method: 论文提出了一种诊断与多样化工具——激活移植（activation grafting）。该方法在贪婪解码的基础上，对残差流施加五个轻量级的扰动，通过确定性的多路径（six-chain deterministic regime）而非随机采样来测试模型能力。研究者利用该方法在八个自由形式的数学数据集（GSM8K 和 MATH）上，对 pass@k=0% 的样本进行恢复测试，并通过 Jaccard 系数验证了不同扰动方式在机制上的差异性。

Result: 实验结果显示，在所测试的八个数学数据集上，10.3% 到 22.9% 的“无法解决（pass@k=0%）”样本，可以通过激活移植的确定性多路径机制成功求解。与之对比，单纯的贪婪解码求解率最高不超过 6%。这证明了这些困难样本在模型的残差流中是结构性可识别的，现有的 pass@k 指标显著低估了模型在极端困难任务上的潜力。

Conclusion: 论文得出结论：现有的 pass@k 指标在衡量极难数学问题时存在盲区，无法准确反映模型的能力上限。通过对残差流进行微小的激活移植（activation grafting）扰动，即使是模型本身无法通过随机采样解决的问题，也可以被确定性的多路径机制解出。这表明模型内部已经编码了解决这些问题的能力，只是无法通过标准的推理路径激发。

Abstract: Math and science reasoning benchmarks rely on pass@k, the fraction of sampled chains that reach gold, as the canonical per-example difficulty signal. The same signal drives RL with verifiable rewards, math data curation, synthetic curricula, and verifier training. We show this proxy has a persistent blind spot on its hardest stratum: on the eight free-form math cells we test (GSM8K and MATH across four open-weight models), 10.3-22.9% of the examples that no sampling seed solves in six tries are instead solved at matched compute by a six-chain deterministic regime. These are greedy decoding plus five cheap residual-stream perturbations applied via activation grafting, while greedy alone solves at most 6% on these math cells. Recovery scales with the additional budget, across perturbations whose mechanistic distinctness we verify across all twelve cells (cross-kind fix-set Jaccard <= 0.47 in every setup). Activation grafting is used as an intervention on internal representations, not a decoding method; we use it purely as a diagnostic and diversification tool, and our recovered items show that the pass@k= 0 % stratum is structurally identifiable in the residual stream rather than that the unmodified model reaches them under ordinary inference.

</details>


### [101] [Convex training of Lipschitz-regularized shallow neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19652)
*Chao Yin,Antoine Lesage-Landry*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将非凸 Lipschitz 正则化神经网络训练转化为凸优化问题的创新方法，实现了全局最优解的快速求解，从而在保证模型精度的同时，显著增强了神经网络对抗攻击的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经网络训练方法往往面临非凸优化带来的局部极小值问题，且在对抗攻击环境下表现脆弱。作者旨在通过数学上更严谨的凸优化方法，在保证训练效率的同时，提升浅层神经网络的 Lipschitz 连续性和对抗鲁棒性。

Method: 提出了一种针对浅层神经网络的训练过程：将原本的非凸 Lipschitz 正则化训练问题转化为一个易于求解的凸限制（convex restriction）问题。该方法既可作为一种独立训练策略，也可作为预训练模型的后处理优化步骤，通过凸优化保证找到不劣于初始解的最优网络参数。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在回归任务中表现优异，相比现有方法，该方案能更有效地降低 Lipschitz 正则化目标函数值。同时，在多个真实数据集上的测试证明，通过此方法训练的网络在保持高预测精度的前提下，对对抗攻击具有更强的防御能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种通过凸优化手段提升浅层神经网络对抗鲁棒性的有效框架。通过将非凸 Lipschitz 正则化训练问题转化为可全局求解的凸限制问题，不仅在理论上保证了性能不劣于初始模型，还在实际应用中证明了其在回归任务中能够显著提升模型的精度与鲁棒性。

Abstract: In this work, we introduce a training procedure for shallow neural networks that promotes robustness against adversarial attacks. We solve a non-convex Lipschitz-regularized training program by introducing a convex restriction that can be efficiently solved to global optimality. Our approach can be employed as a post-processing step by taking a pre-trained network as an initial solution to then solving the convex program whose optimal network is guaranteed to be no worse than the initial one. We illustrate the improvements of our training procedure with experiments using real world datasets for regression tasks under an adversarial setting. We show numerically that solving our proposed convex program yields networks with lower objective values on the Lipschitz-regularized program compared to existing methods. Additionally, we show that on certain datasets, networks obtained using our convex training program are both more accurate and robust with respect to adversarial attacks.

### [102] [LOKI: Memory-Free Null-Space Constrained Lifelong Knowledge Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19679)
*Masih Eskandar,Miquel Sirera Perelló,Stratis Ioannidis,Jennifer Dy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 LOKI，一种无需访问历史数据的终身知识编辑方法，通过动态选择更新层并利用零空间投影技术，在提升新知识获取精度的同时有效缓解了灾难性遗忘。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的终身知识编辑方法存在两大痛点：一是为所有样本固定修改相同的层，导致灵活性差且容易引发灾难性遗忘；二是通常依赖于访问历史数据或进行繁琐的数据统计预处理，这在实际应用中往往难以实现。

Method: 1. 基于希尔伯特-施密特独立性准则（HSIC）的动态层选择机制，根据输入样本灵活选择需要更新的网络层；2. 将梯度更新投影到模型权重的零空间（Null-space）中，从而在不影响旧知识的前提下完成新知识的写入，无需存储或访问历史数据。

Result: 在多项实验中，LOKI 均表现出优于现有方法的性能，平均准确率最高提升了 14%。

Conclusion: LOKI 通过动态层选择和零空间投影技术，成功解决了大语言模型在终身知识编辑中面临的灵活性不足和灾难性遗忘问题，无需访问历史数据即可实现高效更新，并在多项指标上显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Lifelong knowledge editing aims to efficiently and sequentially update language models over time, as new knowledge becomes available or when the model makes mistakes, while preserving acceptable performance on past knowledge. One unresolved challenge is that existing methods modify a fixed set of layers for all new knowledge samples, reducing flexibility and increasing catastrophic forgetting. Another is requiring access to previous knowledge and extensive pre-processing to obtain data statistics. To address these challenges, we introduce LOKI, a novel approach that uses dynamic layer selection based on the Hilbert-Schmidt Independence Criterion and projects gradient updates onto the null-space of the model weights, bypassing the requirement for previous knowledge access. We show that LOKI achieves superior performance to existing approaches across a wide variety of experiments, achieving up to a 14\% improvement in average accuracy.

These representations are transformed into a dynamic semantic graph, where entities and their relationships are modeled by using graph embeddings enhanced by attention mechanisms for capturing both local relevance and global contextual dependencies. Subsequently, an adaptive multi-agent reinforcement learning strategy leverages the attention-aware semantic states to optimize personalized web actions like content recommendation, navigation optimization, and service adaptation. Finally, the continuous online feedback is further integrated to update graph representations and learning policies in real time by ensuring sustained adaptability and performance. The proposed MGAR-WIES acheived better results in terms of accuracy (80%) when compared with existing approaches.

### [104] [Efficiently Representing Algorithms With Chain-of-Thought Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19697)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的理论研究多基于图灵机模型证明思维链（CoT）Transformer的计算能力，但图灵机模型在算法设计和效率分析上不够直观且效率偏低。研究者旨在探讨：CoT Transformer能否以更符合算法分析标准的Word RAM模型为基准，实现高效的计算模拟，从而弥补现有理论与实际算法效率分析之间的鸿沟。

Method: 研究者通过将Word RAM模型（具备随机访问内存和单位代价操作的计算模型）映射到Transformer架构上，分析了三种设置：1. 具有多对数宽度和特定注意力机制的有限精度Transformer；2. 连续思维链（向量形式推理）；3. 混合架构（Transformer层叠加循环神经网络层）。研究评估了这些模型在模拟Word RAM指令集时的开销和复杂度。

Result: 研究表明，在上述三种设置下，CoT Transformer均能以多对数级别的开销高效模拟任何Word RAM算法。对于“平坦”指令集，开销可降至对数平方级；若为无乘法平坦指令集，开销仅为对数级。这一结果显著优于目前已知基于图灵机的模拟方案（后者在Word RAM之上需要二次方级别的开销）。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了思维链（CoT）Transformer不仅在理论上具备图灵完备性，而且能够以多对数（poly-logarithmic）级别的开销高效模拟Word RAM模型。这为理解推理模型的能力边界提供了更切合实际算法分析的理论框架，指出了Transformer作为高效算法执行器的潜力。

Abstract: The increasing popularity of \emph{reasoning} models -- language models that output a series of reasoning or thought tokens before producing an answer -- is justified, in part, by theoretical results showing that chain-of-thought (CoT) transformers can simulate Turing machines, and thus perform arbitrary computation. However, the Turing machine, while suitable for complexity-theoretic analysis, is not convenient, intuitive, or efficient for discussing algorithms. Algorithms are typically designed and analyzed at a higher level of abstraction, captured by the \emph{Word RAM} model with random-access memory and unit-cost operations on $\bigO(\log n)$-bit words. As a result, Word RAM algorithms can be substantially more efficient than their Turing machine counterparts, raising the question: \emph{Can CoT transformers efficiently simulate Word RAM algorithms?} For instance, can they sort $n$ items in $\bigO(n \log n)$ steps or run Dijkstra's algorithm in $\bigO(E + V \log V)$ steps? We answer affirmatively, up to poly-logarithmic overhead. We first establish this for finite-precision transformers with poly-logarithmic width and rightmost unique hard attention, then strengthen the result to two more practical settings with finite width and log-precision: \emph{continuous} CoT, where reasoning takes the form of vectors rather than tokens, and a \emph{hybrid} architecture in which transformer layers sit atop a recurrent (linear RNN) layer. In all three cases, we find that CoT \emph{can} efficiently simulate any Word RAM algorithm with only a poly-logarithmic overhead in $n$. This overhead reduces to log-square when the Word RAM has a ``flat'' instruction set, and only logarithmic for multiplication-free flat instructions -- in stark contrast to known CoT simulations of Turing machines, which require quadratic overhead over Word RAM.

</details>


### [105] [Efficient Neural Network Model Selection for Few-Class Application Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19712)

Method: 本文提出了一种基于数据集属性的“少量类别独特性”（few-class distinctiveness）度量指标，用于评估分类难度。通过该指标，研究者可以在不进行重复训练和测试的情况下直接评估模型与数据集的匹配度，并基于此将模型规模进一步压缩，以适应资源受限的硬件环境。

Result: 该指标使得模型与数据集的比较速度比传统的重复训练测试快 6 到 29 倍。在实际应用中，研究者成功构建了比现有最小模型（如 YOLOv5-nano）更小的模型（体积减小可达 42%），且在保持原有精度的前提下，显著提升了在移动机器人、无人机及物联网设备上的运行效率。

Conclusion: 在少量类别任务中，传统的模型选择方法效率低下。本文提出的基于数据集特征的分类难度指标，能够有效辅助模型选择，在移动机器人、无人机和物联网等资源受限场景下，实现了性能与效率的平衡，证明了针对特定任务属性优化模型选择的必要性。

Abstract: While much effort has focused on developing and benchmarking high-performance neural networks, less attention has been given to how dataset properties, known to practitioners, can guide efficient model selection. Neural models are typically evaluated on datasets with thousands of classes, yet many real-world applications involve fewer than ten. To address this understudied but common setting, we develop a measure of classification difficulty based on data-side properties and show how it enables more efficient model selection for few-class datasets, where traditional approaches are less effective. We term this phenomenon "few-class distinctiveness". Our metric allows comparison of models and datasets 6 to 29$\times$ faster than repeated training and testing. Leveraging this insight, we extend scaled model families below the smallest published models, achieving greater efficiency at similar accuracy, for example models up to 42% smaller than YOLOv5-nano for a mobile robot task. Targeting resource-constrained applications, we demonstrate few-class model selection across mobile robot, drone, and IoT scenarios, highlighting practical gains in efficiency without sacrificing performance.

We formalize the federated bilevel performatively stable (FBPS) point under a decoupled-risk perspective and provide sufficient conditions for its existence and uniqueness. We then develop two federated methods to compute the FBPS solution: FBi-RRM, which converges linearly under a contraction condition, and FBi-SGD, a communication-efficient stochastic method based on federated hypergradient estimation with convergence guarantees under diminishing step sizes when sensitivities are sufficiently small. Conclusion: 研究表明，仅依靠题目难度进行采样不足以优化大模型的推理能力。通过引入任务空间的结构化信息（流形结构）和类型感知（类型意识），能够更有效地平衡模型学习过程中的产出、多样性和实用性，从而提升下游任务性能。

Existing adaptive curriculum learning methods typically prioritize prompts of intermediate difficulty, treating problem selection as a standard bandit problem with independent arms and overlooking the structured, heterogeneous nature of the task space. In this work, we frame problem sampling as a manifold-structured bandit problem with endogenous non-stationarity: problems are related through the model's latent representation space, and sampling decisions can steer how learning signals evolve across that space. To operationalize this perspective, we introduce Bayesian Manifold Curriculum (BMC), a structure-aware framework that organizes problems into a hierarchical task tree and applies Bayesian learning to guide sampling. Empirically, we find that different sampling strategies induce non-trivial tradeoffs between productivity (learning signal), diversity (coverage of the task manifold), and utility (evaluation relevance). These results show that prioritizing difficulty alone is insufficient for strong downstream performance, highlighting the importance of incorporating structure and type-awareness into problem sampling.

Abstract: Partial differential equations (PDEs) play a central role in modeling complex physical, biological, and engineering systems. To bridge this gap, this article proposes the Physics-Informed Broad Learning System (PIBLS), a novel backpropagation-free framework that reformulates PDE solving as a direct least-squares optimization. Abstract: We propose an information-theoretic framework for graph novelty generation, which aims to generate data that are distinct from existing patterns while preserving global structural consistency. Specifically, novelty is enforced by requiring generated samples to be poorly explained by all existing mixture components, while reliability constrains their impact on the overall mixture structure under the Minimum Description Length (MDL) principle. We provide a theoretical analysis showing that, with appropriate threshold choices, the probabilities of misclassifying non-novel or unreliable samples converge to zero with explicit rates. Experiments on synthetic and benchmark graph datasets demonstrate that the proposed method enables principled novelty generation with quantifiable risk.

### [111] [Flow Map Denoisers: Traversing the Distortion-Perception Plane for Inverse Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19802)
*Nicolas Zilberstein,Morteza Mardani,Santiago Segarra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用流图模型（flow map models）的方法，通过单一预训练模型中的一个“前瞻”控制参数，实现了图像修复中保真度与感知质量（DP 前沿）的连续、灵活调节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图像修复中存在一个根本性的权衡：最小化误差的方法往往导致图像模糊，而最大化感知质量的方法虽图像清晰但保真度下降。现有的方法通常只能锁定在这一权衡曲线上的单一工作点，或者需要繁琐的配对数据监督、辅助模型或针对不同采样器的参数调整，难以灵活地在保真度和感知质量之间进行切换。

Method: 研究人员利用流匹配（flow matching）的扩展——流图模型，定义了一个隐式的去噪器家族。通过引入“前瞻”参数 t，将其作为控制旋钮，在无需额外辅助模型或复杂的超参数调整的情况下，跨越从最小均方误差（MMSE）到感知质量驱动的 DP 前沿。该方法被集成到即插即用（Plug-and-Play）求解器中，以解决通用的逆问题。

Result: 在 Gaussian 目标下，理论证明了该方法能精确复现最优 DP 前沿；在自然图像实验（CelebA 和 AFHQ 数据集）中，该方法在多种线性和非线性逆问题上，仅凭单个预训练模型即可匹配甚至超越专门针对特定权衡点设计的基准方法。

Conclusion: 本文证明了流图模型（flow map models）可以通过单一的训练模型，通过简单的“前瞻”（lookahead）参数调节，在失真-感知（DP）权衡曲线上实现连续调节。这一发现简化了图像修复任务中感知质量与保真度之间的平衡控制，且无需针对不同需求重新训练模型。

Abstract: Image restoration faces a fundamental tradeoff: methods that minimize error produce blurry reconstructions, while those that maximize perceptual quality yield sharp but less faithful images. Existing approaches either commit to a single operating point on this distortion perception (DP) frontier or require paired-data supervision, auxiliary models, or hyperparameter tuning of the sampler to access different points. We show that flow map models, a recent extension of flow matching for few-step sampling that learns an average field, implicitly define a one-parameter family of denoisers that continuously spans the DP frontier. The lookahead parameter t acts as a control knob between the MMSE and perceptual regimes. For Gaussian targets, we prove that varying t exactly recovers the optimal DP frontier; for natural images, we observe similar behavior empirically. Within a Plug-and-Play solver, the same mechanism extends to general inverse problems, where it controls a tradeoff between perceptual alignment and data consistency. Despite the lack of exact optimality guarantees in this setting, a single trained flow map spans the DP tradeoff, matching or exceeding specialized baselines at both extremes. Extensive experiments on CelebA ($128\times 128$) and AFHQ ($256\times 256$) across several linear and nonlinear inverse tasks validate our findings.

### [112] [Uncertainty-Aware Reward Modeling for Stable RLHF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19818)
*Licheng Pan,Haocheng Yang,Haoxuan Li,Yichen Sun,Yunsheng Lu,Shijian Wang,Lei Shen,Yuan Lu,Zhixuan Chu,Hao Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 RLHF 流程中存在两个核心缺陷：一是奖励模型作为确定性点估计器，无法预警其预测的不确定性；二是 GRPO 等策略优化算法倾向于放大不可靠的奖励信号。这导致策略探索过程中模型极易通过奖励欺骗手段获取高分，降低了对齐质量。

Method: 提出“不确定性感知奖励建模（UARM）”方法。具体包括：1. 利用基于分位数的共形预测（Quantile-based Conformal Prediction）为奖励模型提供校准后的不确定性估计；2. 通过异方差方差分解（Heteroscedastic Variance Decomposition）对 GRPO（组相对策略优化）的优势函数进行加权，从而降低不可靠奖励信号的权重。

Result: 在 HelpSteer、UltraFeedback 和 PKU-SafeRLHF 等数据集上的实验表明，UARM 显著提升了奖励模型的校准效果，有效抑制了奖励欺骗现象，并在对齐质量上优于标准 GRPO 及其他不考虑不确定性的基线方法。

Conclusion: UARM 通过引入不确定性感知机制，有效解决了强化学习中奖励模型不可靠导致奖励欺骗（Reward Hacking）的问题，为大语言模型的对齐提供了一种更鲁棒、更精准的优化框架。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) aligns large language models by training reward models on preference data and optimizing policies to maximize predicted rewards. However, this pipeline faces two fundamental challenges: (1) reward models cannot signal when their predictions are unreliable, since they usually act as deterministic point estimators; and (2) modern group-based policy optimization can amplify unreliable reward signals, as exemplified by GRPO's uniform treatment of rewards during advantage computation. As policies explore increasingly diverse responses, these two limitations create a critical vulnerability: unreliable reward estimates may be granted disproportionate influence, triggering severe reward hacking. We propose Uncertainty-Aware Reward Modeling (UARM), which equips reward models with calibrated uncertainty via quantile-based conformal prediction and reweights GRPO advantages through heteroscedastic variance decomposition. Experiments across HelpSteer, UltraFeedback, and PKU-SafeRLHF demonstrate that UARM significantly improves reward model calibration, reduces reward hacking, and enhances downstream alignment quality compared to standard GRPO and uncertainty-agnostic baselines.

</details>

*Maryam Sanisales,Zahed Rahmati,Ali Darvishi Boloorani,Ali Vefghi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将邻近图与图神经网络结合的新方法，用于更精准地预测尘源排放，通过构建有效的空间结构，该方法在时空动态建模方面显著优于传统的LSTM模型和基于随机图的GNN模型。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 沙尘暴对环境和健康危害巨大，传统的预测方法难以准确捕捉沙尘源排放过程中的复杂时空动态依赖关系，因此需要引入更强大的时空建模工具。

Method: 研究提出了利用多种邻近图（Delaunay三角剖分、Gabriel图、k-近邻图和Yao图）作为图神经网络（包括GraphSAGE、GCN和GAT）的输入结构，通过图上的消息传递机制来建模地理空间数据的复杂关系。同时，通过与随机图构建的GNN进行对照实验，验证了空间结构表达的必要性。

Result: 实验结果表明，采用邻近图结构的GNN模型在尘源排放预测任务中表现优异，不仅显著优于使用随机图的GNN模型，在预测精度上也远超传统的长短期记忆网络（LSTM）。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了邻近图与图神经网络（GNN）的结合是处理尘源排放预测任务的有效范式，能够显著提升模型对复杂时空动态的捕捉能力，为环境灾害预警提供了一种优于传统循环神经网络（如LSTM）的新方法。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of dust source emissions is critical for mitigating the significant environmental and health hazards posed by dust storms. Traditional forecasting methods often struggle to capture the complex spatiotemporal dynamics of these phenomena.
  In this paper, we demonstrate that proximity graphs enable Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) to effectively model the intricate spatial and temporal relationships between data points. Specifically, we use proximity graphs--such as Delaunay triangulation, Gabriel graph, k-Nearest Neighbor graph, and Yao graph--as the input for GNNs (including GraphSAGE, Graph Convolutional Networks, and Graph Attention Networks) to perform message passing.
  Our approach highlights the effectiveness of integrating proximity graphs with GNNs for robust and accurate dust source forecasting. To emphasize the importance of proximity graph representations, we compare our method against GNNs using random graphs for message passing. The results show that GNNs with proximity graphs significantly outperform those with random graphs and are also far superior to Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) model in dust source emission forecasting.

*Daehwan Kim,Haejun Chung,Ikbeom Jang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对医疗表格数据标注昂贵及现有自监督方法离散化策略僵化的问题，本文提出“Adaptive Binning”方法，通过训练自适应的从粗到细离散化策略及异构感知目标函数，实现了医疗表格表示学习的性能提升，并建立了标准化评估基准。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗表格数据在临床研究中极为常见，但由于人工标注成本高昂，深度学习在处理此类数据时应用受限。现有的基于分箱（binning）的自监督学习方法通常采用全局固定的分位数离散化，且忽略了特征间的异构性，限制了模型捕捉复杂数据结构的能力。因此，需要一种能够利用无标签数据、并根据训练过程动态调整离散化方式的机制。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为“自适应分箱”（Adaptive Binning）的训练自适应离散化自监督学习（SSL）框架。其核心思想是将离散化与模型训练相结合，采用基于特征的“从粗到细”的学习课程。该方法在损失函数平稳时逐步细化离散化粒度，并结合表征意识（representation-aware）的分割策略，同时统一了类别特征的重建和数值特征的序数监督。此外，研究还构建了一个包含标准化协议的医疗表格SSL基准测试集。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的Adaptive Binning方法通过自适应、从粗到细的离散化策略，有效克服了传统自监督学习在医疗表格数据中应用时存在的局限性。该方法无需针对具体数据集进行繁琐的离散化调优，能够显著提升模型在医疗表格任务上的表征能力，为医疗表格数据的自监督学习提供了通用且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Medical tabular data are ubiquitous in clinical research, but deep learning for tables remains underexplored because reliable labels often require costly expert adjudication, even though structured clinical variables are routinely available in tabular form. Self-supervised learning can leverage these unlabeled tables, and recent binning-based pretexts offer a promising inductive bias, but existing objectives fix a single global quantile discretization and apply feature-agnostic supervision. We propose Adaptive Binning, a training-adaptive discretization pretext for tabular SSL that couples discretization to learning through a feature-wise coarse-to-fine curriculum. Motivated by the spectral bias of neural networks and the principles of curriculum learning, our method progressively refines discretization per feature upon plateau detection and selects representation-aware splits to jointly improve value-space concentration and representation-space coherence. A heterogeneity-aware objective unifies categorical reconstruction with ordinal supervision for numerical features, and experiments on public medical tabular datasets under unified evaluation protocols show consistent gains for linear probing and fine-tuning without dataset-specific discretization tuning. We further introduce a medical tabular SSL benchmark with standardized protocols to support reproducible progress in this underexplored domain. Our code is available at https://github.com/labhai/Adaptive-Binning.

However, when using two-input NNs to consider feature interactions or when applying them to high-dimensional datasets, training NAM and NBM becomes intractable due to the increase in the computational resources required. This paper proposes incorporating the feature selection mechanism into NAM and NBM to resolve computational bottlenecks. We introduce the feature selection layer in both models and update the selection weights during training. Our method is simple and can reduce computational costs and model sizes compared to vanilla NAM and NBM. In addition, it enables us to use two-input NNs even in high-dimensional datasets and capture feature interactions. We demonstrate that the proposed models are computationally efficient compared to vanilla NAM and NBM, and they exhibit better or comparable performance with state-of-the-art GAMs.

Abstract: We introduce SEA-PINN, a novel architecture that incorporates a Squeeze-Excitation-like attention mechanism into physics-informed neural networks to dynamically recalibrate the importance of neurons across layers. A key feature of SEA-PINN is its highly stable initialization. Notably, without employing Fourier feature embeddings or periodic activation functions, SEA-PINN attained competitive accuracy (83\% vs. 90\% improvement relative to FNN-PINN on the high-frequency case 7) as compared with TSA-PINN-a model specifically engineered for high-frequency problems via learnable frequencies in sinusoidal activations. Furthermore, integrating SEA-PINN into TSA-PINN boosted performance by 42.49\%. ### [117] [Global Convergence of Gradient Descent for Score Matching in Gaussian Mixtures via Reverse Fisher Divergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19876)
*Alexander Tyurin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文研究了反向 Fisher 散度在拟合高斯混合模型（GMM）中的优化表现，证明了相比传统的前向 Fisher 散度，反向 Fisher 散度具有更优的优化地形，能够实现从随机初始化到全局最优的收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现代生成模型（如扩散模型）中，常用的前向 Fisher 散度在训练过程中存在收敛行为不理想、依赖初始化等问题，即便是简单的模型也可能难以收敛到全局最优解。为了解决这一优化困境，论文旨在探索并证明使用反向 Fisher 散度作为训练目标是否能带来更好的优化性质。

Method: 通过理论分析和梯度下降（GD）动力学研究，对比了前向与反向 Fisher 散度的优化特性。对于单高斯教师模型，证明了在学生模型为固定权重和单位协方差的高斯混合模型时，GD 可从任意初始化点全局收敛；对于 GMM 教师模型，在均值满足特定分离度（$\widetilde{\Omega}(1)$-separation）和随机初始化的条件下，证明了学生模型各分量能收敛至对应的教师分量，并给出了总变差距离（TV distance）下的收敛保证。利用了基于 Lyapunov 函数的分析方法来刻画优化过程。

Result: 研究表明，使用反向 Fisher 散度能够使梯度下降算法避开前向 Fisher 散度带来的不良收敛区域。理论上证明了在特定条件下，梯度下降可以实现从随机初始化到全局最优的收敛，克服了优化地形中的局部极小值或不良鞍点问题，保证了学生分布在总变差距离意义下的有效逼近。

Conclusion: 研究证明，反向 Fisher 散度通过改变优化目标，显著改善了高斯混合模型（GMM）拟合过程中的优化地形。相比前向 Fisher 散度，反向 Fisher 散度在梯度下降中表现出更强的鲁棒性和全局收敛性，为生成模型和统计建模提供了更优的训练目标。

Abstract: The score matching problem is a central training objective in modern generative modeling, diffusion models, fitting unnormalized statistical models, and inverse problems. A standard approach is to minimize the forward Fisher divergence, where the expectation is taken with respect to the teacher distribution. However, recent results show that even in simple Gaussian mixture model settings, this objective can lead to undesirable and initialization-dependent convergence behavior. In this paper, we study an alternative objective: the reverse Fisher divergence, where the expectation is taken with respect to the student distribution. We analyze gradient descent (GD) for fitting Gaussian mixture models and show that this change in the objective leads to significantly better optimization properties. First, when the teacher distribution is a single Gaussian and the student is a Gaussian mixture model with fixed weights and identity covariances, we prove the global convergence of GD from arbitrary initializations. Second, we extend the analysis to the case where the teacher is also a Gaussian mixture model and prove global convergence guarantees under a global random initialization scheme and a $\widetildeΩ(1)$-separation assumption on the target means. In particular, with high probability, each student component converges near its closest teacher component, and we provide conditions under which the student distribution converges in total variation distance. Our proofs rely on a new Lyapunov-based analysis of the gradient descent dynamics, showing that the reverse Fisher divergence has a much more favorable optimization landscape than the forward Fisher divergence.

### [118] [On the Oracle Complexity of Interpolation-Based Gradient Descent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19878)
*Dongmin Lee,William Lu,Anuran Makur*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型不精确梯度优化算法 PPI-GD，通过对数据域进行分段多项式插值来近似全梯度，在保持高效率的同时，利用数据平滑性在关键设置下超越了传统的梯度下降方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的一阶优化方法通常依赖于参数平滑性，但近期的研究指出，利用经验风险最小化（ERM）中数据损失函数的平滑性可以显著提高梯度下降（GD）的预言机复杂度。本文旨在开发一种能够有效利用这种数据平滑性来降低计算开销的新型优化算法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“分段多项式插值梯度下降”（PPI-GD）的不精确梯度方法。该方法通过在数据域的等距点查询一阶预言机，对梯度样本进行分段多项式插值，从而在每次迭代中近似全梯度。此外，作者将双三次样条插值的误差分析技术推广至 d 变量张量积多项式插值。

Result: 在强凸和非凸损失函数下，当数据空间维度受限于训练样本数量的多对数函数时，PPI-GD 在特定场景下表现出比多种 GD 变体更优的预言机复杂度。此外，论文完善了关于 d 变量张量积多项式插值的理论误差分析。

Conclusion: PPI-GD 算法通过利用数据空间的平滑性，为一阶优化提供了一种高效的梯度近似方法。该研究不仅在特定条件下实现了优于现有梯度下降变体的预言机复杂度，还为高维张量积多项式插值的误差分析提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Recent work on first-order optimizers for empirical risk minimization (ERM) has suggested that smoothness of ERM loss functions in the training data, rather than in the optimization parameters, can be leveraged to improve the oracle complexity of gradient descent (GD) methods. In this paper, we propose an inexact gradient method, piecewise polynomial interpolation-based gradient descent (PPI-GD), which approximates the full gradient in each iteration by querying the first-order oracle at equidistant points in the data domain to construct polynomial interpolants of the resulting gradient samples over appropriately sized patches of the data domain. We analyze the oracle complexity of PPI-GD for strongly convex and non-convex loss functions when the data space dimension is bounded by a polylogarithmic function of the number of training samples, and find it to outperform several GD variants in key regimes when the loss function is sufficiently smooth. Furthermore, our analysis extends several techniques from the error analysis of bicubic spline interpolants to the setting of $d$-variate tensor product polynomial interpolants which may be of independent interest in interpolation analysis.

### [119] [Matching Markets meet Cumulative Prospect Theory: Towards Optimal and Adversarially Robust Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19883)
*Ananya Kunisetty,Avishek Ghosh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了受累积前景理论（CPT）约束的多智能体匹配市场问题，通过引入风险敏感决策模型并优化探索策略，在标准及对抗性环境中均实现了对数级最优后悔保证，有效解决了大规模动作空间下的决策效率问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的强化学习模型通常假设代理是理性经济人，但现实中的人类决策往往表现出风险敏感性和非线性偏好。本文旨在建立一个能捕捉人类行为特征的多智能体匹配模型，并在处理大规模臂空间及对抗性奖励污染时，提供具有理论保证的学习策略。

Method: 1. 将累积前景理论（CPT）及其非线性权重函数集成到多智能体多臂老虎机模型中，以模拟人类的行为偏好。
2. 对现有学习算法进行改进，通过精心设计活跃臂集合（active set of arms）的筛选机制，消除了对最小偏好间隙的强依赖。
3. 针对奖励受到污染的对抗性市场，提出了具备鲁棒性的学习算法，分别涵盖了已知和未知污染预算的情境。

Result: 1. 在标准CPT设置下，获得了玩家最优后悔界 $\mathcal{O}(K\log T (\frac{1}{Δ})^{2/α})$。
2. 通过改进策略，在臂数量 $K$ 远大于玩家数量 $N$ 的情况下，实现了对数级最优后悔保证，去除了主导项中对 $K$ 的依赖。
3. 在对抗性市场中，针对已知和未知污染预算的情况，均建立并验证了对数级的玩家最优后悔界。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入累积前景理论（CPT）有效建模了人类在双边匹配市场中的决策行为，并证明了在标准及对抗环境下，通过优化探索策略可以实现对数级玩家最优后悔保证。这为理解风险敏感型代理在复杂多智能体系统中的行为提供了强有力的理论框架。

Abstract: We study a multi-agent multi-armed bandit problem in the competitive setup with two-sided matching markets under a human centric decision making model. To capture human preferences, we use cumulative prospect theory (CPT) that weighs the actions of the agent in a nonlinear fashion using a ($α$-Hölder continuous) weight function. CPT has been widely used in behavioral economics and risk sensitive machine learning to emulate human preferences. We analyze the state-of-the-art learning algorithm with CPT weight distorted rewards and obtain a player optimal regret of $\mathcal{O}(K\log T \left(\frac{1}Δ\right)^{2/α})$, where $K$ denotes the number of arms, $T$ is the learning horizon, and $Δ$ represents (suitably defined) players' minimum preference gap. Noticing the dependence on $Δ$ to be sub-optimal, we further improve this regret by judiciously selecting the active set of arms during exploration, which removes the dependence on $K$ in the dominant term and achieves an improved (optimal) regret guarantees in the setting where the number of arms $K$ is significantly larger than the number of players $N$. In addition, we consider adversarial markets where the observed rewards of the agents may be corrupted. We propose and analyze algorithms for robust markets with CPT as risk sensitive measure in both settings where the total corruption budget is known and where it is unknown, and establish logarithmic player-optimal regret guarantees in both cases.

</details>


### [120] [SL-S4Wave: Self-Supervised Learning of Physiological Waveforms with Structured State Space Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19888)

Conclusion: 本研究提出的SL-S4Wave框架通过结合自监督对比学习与多尺度结构化状态空间模型，有效解决了医疗时间序列中长距离依赖捕捉困难、噪声干扰以及标注数据稀缺的问题，为处理复杂的生理信号提供了一种高效且鲁棒的新范式。

Abstract: Modeling long-sequence medical time series data, such as electrocardiograms (ECG), poses significant challenges due to high sampling rates, multichannel signal complexity, inherent noise, and limited labeled data. While recent self-supervised learning (SSL) methods, based on various encoder architectures such as convolutional neural networks, have been proposed to learn representations from unlabeled data, they often fall short in capturing long-range dependencies and noise-invariant features. Structured state space models (S4) excel at long-sequence modeling, but existing S4 architectures fail to capture the unique characteristics of multichannel physiological waveforms. In this work, we propose SL-S4Wave, a self-supervised learning framework that combines contrastive learning with a tailored encoder built on structured state space models. The encoder incorporates multi-layer global convolution using multiscale subkernels, enabling the capture of both fine-grained local patterns and long-range temporal dependencies in noisy, high-resolution multichannel waveforms. Extensive experiments on real-world datasets demonstrate that SL-S4Wave (1) consistently outperforms state-of-the-art supervised and self-supervised baselines in a challenging arrhythmia detection task, (2) achieves high performance with significantly fewer labeled examples, showcasing strong label efficiency, and (3) maintains robust performance on long waveform segments, highlighting its capacity to model complex temporal dynamics in long sequences that most existing approaches fail to efficiently model, and (4) transfers effectively to unseen arrhythmia types, underscoring its robust cross-domain generalization. We additionally evaluate SL-S4Wave on multiple EEG tasks, achieving superior performance over strong baselines, demonstrating generalizability of our approach beyond cardiac waveforms.

### [121] [Adversarial Bandit Optimization with Globally Bounded Perturbations to Convex Losses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19891)
*Zhuoyu Cheng,Kohei Hatano,Eiji Takimoto*

TL;DR: 本文研究了带有全局扰动预算的对抗性强盗优化问题，将原有的线性损失扩展至凸且$\beta$-光滑损失函数，通过改进算法实现了对扰动下遗憾值的有效控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的对抗性强盗优化研究多局限于线性损失函数，难以应对现实中更为复杂的非凸、非光滑损失函数场景，且在存在全局预算约束的对抗性扰动下，缺乏对一般凸且$\beta$-光滑损失函数的深入分析，因此有必要拓展该框架并量化扰动对后悔值的影响。

Method: 作者通过修改标准的强盗优化（Bandit Optimization）算法，引入了针对对抗性扰动的控制策略，并开发了一种新的分析框架，旨在精确控制由扰动引起的额外遗憾，同时确保在没有扰动的情况下能回归到标准强盗凸优化问题的遗憾界。

Result: 研究为该更广泛的损失函数类建立了预期的遗憾界（Regret Guarantees），并显式地刻画了扰动预算对遗憾值的影响；在无扰动的特殊情况下，该算法的性能与标准强盗凸优化算法的遗憾界一致。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架成功将全局预算下的对抗性扰动模型从线性损失函数扩展到了更广泛的凸且$\beta$-光滑损失函数类。研究证明了该方法在处理非凸、非光滑扰动时的稳健性，并为理解对抗性扰动对遗憾值的影响提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: We study adversarial bandit optimization in which the loss functions may be non-convex and non-smooth. In each round, the learner selects an action and observes only the loss incurred at that action. The loss consists of an underlying convex and $β$-smooth component and an adversarial perturbation that may be chosen after observing the learner's action. The perturbations are subject to a global budget controlling their cumulative magnitude over time.
  This framework extends the globally budgeted, post-action perturbation model from underlying linear losses to general convex and $β$-smooth losses. For this broader class, we establish expected regret guarantees that explicitly characterize the effect of the perturbation budget.
  To establish these guarantees, we modify a standard bandit optimization algorithm and develop an analysis that controls the additional regret caused by the perturbations. In the absence of perturbations, our results reduce to regret guarantees for the standard bandit convex optimization setting with $β$-smooth losses.

### [122] [Score Approximation for Diffusion Models on Arbitrary Low-Dimensional Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19894)
*Xinhe Mu,Zaijiu Shang,Zhaoqi Zhou,Chuan Zhou,Qi Meng,Guiying Yan,Zhiming Ma*

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个通用的得分近似定理，证明了扩散模型无需强平滑假设即可处理复杂分布，通过降低复杂度对环境维度的依赖，解释了扩散模型在处理现实世界不规则数据时的卓越表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散模型理论边界通常依赖于Lipschitz连续性或光滑流形假设，这与现实世界数据（包含奇异点、尖锐边界和不连续聚类）的复杂结构相悖，需要建立更通用的得分近似理论。

Method: 提出了一种新颖的离散混合（discrete-mixture）公式，证明了利用ReLU神经网络可以近似任何支持在任意紧集（紧致集）上且具有上闵可夫维度d的分布的得分函数，并通过该构造避开了环境维度对模型复杂度的指数级影响。

Result: 证明了ReLU神经网络的复杂度仅随数据的上闵可夫维度d呈指数增长，打破了环境维度的诅咒；并结合现有的反向随机微分方程（SDE）求解理论，论证了扩散模型在处理非光滑数据分布时的理论可行性。

Conclusion: 扩散模型具有极强的适应性，能够处理现实世界中不规则、非平滑的数据结构，其泛化能力源于得分网络可以在不依赖强平滑性假设的前提下，有效地近似复杂分布的得分函数。

Abstract: The remarkable success of score-based diffusion models has spurred significant efforts to establish their theoretical foundations. However, existing complexity bounds for score approximation rely heavily on restrictive assumptions like Lipschitz continuous densities or smooth manifold supports, which are routinely violated by the singularities, sharp boundaries, and disjoint clusters inherent to real-world perceptual data. This work establishes a universal score approximation theorem that works for any distribution supported on any compact set of upper Minkowski dimension $d$. Using a novel discrete-mixture formulation, we prove that the score function can be approximated with a ReLU network whose complexity grows exponentially only with $d$, thus breaking the exponential curse of ambient dimensionality. Combined with existing theories on accurately solving the backward diffusion SDE for arbitrary compact distributions, our work shows that diffusion models readily adapt to irregular, non-smooth data structures, explaining their competence in real-world generative tasks.

### [123] [ADaPT: Token-Level Decoupling for Efficient Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19919)
*Tingyun Li,Zishang Jiang,Jinyi Han,Xinyi Wang,Sihang Jiang,Han Xia,Zhaoqian Dai,Shuguang Ma,Fei Yu,Jiaqing Liang,Yanghua Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ADaPT 框架通过引入模式选择标记解耦了推理过程中的效率激励与正确性优化，在大幅降低推理成本的同时维持了大模型的强推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型虽然依赖长思维链（CoT）实现高性能，但均匀的推理深度导致了极高的计算冗余。现有的优化方法往往因将效率惩罚与正确性奖励在序列级耦合，导致在追求效率时损害了模型的正确推理能力。

Method: 提出“自适应双过程思维”（ADaPT）框架。核心在于引入一个特殊的模式选择标记（mode-selection token），在训练时仅对该标记施加效率奖励，从而解耦效率目标与正确性奖励；在推理时通过调节该标记的生成概率，实现对推理深度的灵活控制，从而在帕累托前沿进行平滑调节。

Result: 实验表明，ADaPT 在多个基准测试中均能显著降低推理成本，且在性能与效率的平衡上优于现有方法，实现了单一模型在不同推理深度需求下的自适应切换。

Conclusion: ADaPT 通过在训练阶段解耦效率与正确性信号，成功实现了模型在推理时对性能与成本的动态平衡，证明了在保留大模型强推理能力的同时降低计算成本的可行性。

Abstract: Large reasoning models rely on long chain-of-thought to achieve strong performance, but applying such reasoning uniformly incurs high computational cost. Existing efficiency-oriented methods attempt to shorten or mix reasoning strategies, yet often degrade reasoning capability. We identify the root cause as sequence-level coupling between efficiency incentives and correctness optimization, which implicitly penalizes long but correct reasoning trajectories. To address this issue, we propose Adaptive Dual-Process Thinking (ADaPT), a token-level dual-process framework that explicitly decouples efficiency and correctness signals during training. ADaPT introduces a mode-selection token to control fast and slow reasoning, applying efficiency-related rewards exclusively to this token to avoid penalizing correct long reasoning while encouraging efficiency when appropriate. Moreover, ADaPT enables precise and continuous control over the efficiency-performance trade-off at inference time: by adjusting the generation probability of the mode-selection token, a single trained model can smoothly move along the efficiency-performance Pareto frontier. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ADaPT significantly reduces inference cost while maintaining strong reasoning performance across multiple benchmarks.

### [124] [Compositionality Emerges in a Narrow Depth-Connectivity Regime: Architecture Constraints and Solution Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19941)
*Dat H. Do,Rushi Shah,Duc V. Le,Dianbo Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现神经网络的组合性仅在特定的深度与稀疏连接组合（即“黄金窗口”）中涌现，并提出了相应的剪枝与深度预测技术来显式增强模型的组合泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 组合性（Compositionality）被认为是模型泛化的核心基础，但标准梯度下降训练的模型往往难以形成有效的组合内部结构。现有研究尚不清楚组合性形成的具体条件及其背后的机制，因此该工作旨在探究模型在何种结构条件下能够涌现组合性。

Method: 研究通过实验分析模型在不同稀疏度和深度下的表现，提出了以下两种方法：1. 相似性剪枝（Similarity-based Pruning, SP）：旨在恢复并优化网络的组合连接性；2. 深度预测启发式算法（Heuristic Depth Predictor）：用于预估组合性最可能出现的网络深度。同时，作者构建了一个基于组合稀疏性、体积比论证和特征干扰边界的理论框架来支撑实验发现。

Result: 研究发现组合性的涌现具有严格的限制：1. 在连接性方面，它高度依赖于保留的具体连接，而非简单的权重稀疏度；2. 在深度方面，它仅存在于一个随目标任务变化的狭窄区间内。当不满足这些条件时，梯度下降倾向于收敛到“碎片化”的解而非组合性解。通过所提方法，可以成功提升模型识别和利用组合特征的能力。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了组合性并非神经网络训练的自然属性，而是存在于特定的“深度-连接性”窗口内。通过引入相似性剪枝和深度预测启发式算法，研究者能够有效诱导模型形成组合结构，为理解模型泛化能力提供了新的理论和实践视角。

Abstract: Compositionality is believed to be the foundation for generalization, enabling models to reuse meaningful primitives in novel combinations. Yet, models trained with standard gradient-based optimization rarely, and often only weakly, exhibit compositional internal structure, and it remains unclear how or why such compositionality forms. In this work, we show that compositionality emerges in a narrow connectivity-depth sweet spot. Along the connectivity axis, compositionality only appears in some specifically sparse networks, heavily depends on which connections remain rather than on weights' sparsity alone. Along the depth axis, compositionality emerges within a narrow, target-dependent regime, peaking at specific depths, while both shallower and deeper networks fail. When either the depth or connectivity condition is violated, gradient descent silently converges to fractured solutions rather than compositional ones. To discover and exploit this emergence, we introduce (i) similarity-based pruning (SP) to recover compositional connectivity and (ii) a heuristic depth predictor to estimate where compositionality is most likely to appear. Finally, we support these empirical findings with a theoretical framework based on compositional sparsity, volume-ratio arguments, and feature-interference bounds, explaining why compositional solutions are reachable only in a narrow depth-connectivity regime.

Abstract: Tsetlin Machine (TM) is a logic-based machine learning approach that relies on simple bitwise operations and finite-state automata, which makes it attractive for edge AI deployments. Recent work has focused on co-processor and accelerator designs based on Tsetlin Machines (TMs). Although these designs achieve high performance, they typically depend on tightly coupled interfaces, microcode-style programming, and external host processors, limiting flexibility and ease of programming. In this work, we present a domain-specific RISC-V microprocessor architecture and design flow tailored for TM inference. Leveraging the modular structure of RISC-V, we design a reduced instruction subset processor that retains programmability while targeting improved performance and lower energy consumption for TM workloads. Instruction profiling is employed to guide instruction reduction, followed by datapath and control path simplifications tailored to TM inference. Method: 提出Kolmogorov-Arnold储备池计算（KARC），用基于Kolmogorov-Arnold表示定理的显式基函数展开替代了传统储备池计算中的循环结构，利用KAN的表达能力并通过线性最小二乘法实现高效的闭式解训练。

Result: KARC在多个具有挑战性的基准测试（如偏微分方程）中表现优于现有的储备池计算方法，且在保持相似计算成本的情况下实现了更高的预测精度，并可成功应用于生成式扩散模型。

Conclusion: KARC成功架起了储备池计算与Kolmogorov-Arnold网络之间的桥梁，提供了一种兼具高表达能力、计算效率和闭式解训练优势的新型动力系统预测框架，在复杂任务中展现出卓越的性能。

Abstract: Reservoir computing offers a lightweight framework for forecasting dynamical systems but may struggle to capture long-range dependencies due to limited representational capacity. Conventional reservoir computing recurrently uses trainable reservoirs with hyperparameter sensitivity, while the next-generation reservoir computing removes recurrence at the cost of rapidly growing feature dimensions. Here, we develop Kolmogorov-Arnold Reservoir Computing (KARC), which replaces reservoirs with explicit basis-function expansions inspired by the Kolmogorov-Arnold representation theorem. We rigorously show that KARC is a lightweight design of Kolmogorov-Arnold networks (KANs), preserving the potential expressive capacity of KANs while admitting efficient closed-form training of reservoir computing. At comparable cost, KARC outperforms existing reservoir computing methods on challenging benchmarks including partial differential equations. It can also be integrated with generative diffusion models for text-to-image generation. This work thus establishes a principled bridge between reservoir computing and KANs, enabling efficient and high-fidelity dynamical system forecasting.

</details>


### [128] [Activation- and Influence-Aware Ranks (AIR): Function-Preserving SVD Compression for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19993)
*Nico Harder,Daniel Becking,Karsten Mueller,Wojciech Samek*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AIR 是一种创新的 LLM 压缩框架，通过整合权重的影响力与激活信息，在低秩分解中实现更精确的逼近，显著提升了模型压缩后的性能与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的低秩分解压缩方法（如 SVD-LLM）主要依赖于激活值，往往忽略了各权重在模型输出中的实际重要性（即梯度影响力），导致压缩后的精度损失较大，且需要较多的校准数据。

Method: 提出了一种名为 AIR（Activation- and Influence-Aware Ranks）的压缩框架，基于奇异值分解（SVD）。该方法首先利用激活值进行初步近似，随后通过单次闭式交替最小二乘法（ALS）优化，并将反向传播的梯度影响力（Influence）引入权重的低秩逼近过程中，确保在单调下降的条件下优化精度。

Result: 实验表明，AIR 在保留 60% 参数的情况下，困惑度（Perplexity）比 SVD-LLM 提高了 18% 以上；在仅使用 10% 校准数据的情况下即可达到同等性能；此外，它还能显著减少计算浮点运算量（FLOPs）、峰值内存使用及每 token 延迟。

Conclusion: AIR 框架证明了通过结合激活值与反向传播的影响力信息，可以更有效地对大语言模型进行低秩分解压缩。该方法在显著降低参数量的同时，能维持高质量的模型性能，且在实际硬件部署中表现出优异的计算效率。

Abstract: We present Activation- and Influence-Aware Ranks (AIR), an SVD-based LLM compression framework that guides each weight matrix's low-rank approximation with a backward-signal influence metric. Starting from the activation-aware optimum of SVD-LLM(W), AIR runs a single closed-form alternating least squares (ALS) sweep that integrates influence element-wise under a monotone-descent guarantee. AIR is layer-local and composes orthogonally with end-to-end methods: alone it exceeds ACIP, and AIR+LoRA outperforms it further. AIR improves perplexity over SVD-LLM(W) by >18% at <=60% parameter retention, matches its quality with ~90% less calibration data, and turns parameter savings into FLOP, peak-memory, and per-token latency gains.

</details>


### [129] [Connect the Dots: Training LLMs for Long-Lifecycle Agents with Cross-Domain Generalization Via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20002)

Method: 1. 设计了包含任务解决与上下文更新交替的长滚动序列的端到端强化学习（RL）算法及基础设施；2. 开发了专门用于激发和评估LLM该元能力的训练任务与环境；3. 采用了类似GRPO的强化学习算法，并引入了细粒度的信用分配机制。

Abstract: This work presents a general framework for training large language models (LLMs) to "Connect the Dots" (CoD), a meta-capability required by long-lifecycle agents: as an LLM-based AI agent gets deployed in an environment, it solves a long sequence of tasks while continuously exploring the environment, learning from its own experiences, and iteratively self-updating its context about the environment, thereby achieving progressively better performance on future tasks conditioned on the updated context. Major components of the CoD framework include: (1) algorithm design and infrastructure for end-to-end reinforcement learning (RL) with long rollout sequences interleaving solve-task and update-context episodes; (2) tasks and environments for incentivizing and eliciting the targeted meta-capability in LLMs during training, as well as for faithfully measuring progress during evaluation. We present proof-of-concept implementations of the CoD framework, including a GRPO-style RL algorithm with fine-grained credit assignment, as well as tasks and environments tailored to the targeted meta-capability (rather than domain-specific LLM capabilities or standard task-by-task RL). Empirical results validate the efficacy of end-to-end RL training in the CoD setting, and demonstrate the potential for out-of-distribution generalization -- within the training domains, across different domains, and from CoD to Ralph-loop settings -- of the elicited meta-capability. Our investigation of CoD connects several lines of prior works, and opens up new opportunities for advancing LLMs and AI agents. To facilitate further research and applications, we release our implementations at \url{https://github.com/agentscope-ai/Trinity-RFT/tree/research/cod/examples/research_cod}.
